The Beijing Municipal Party Department has been ordered to lead all circles in preparing for publicity. It is heard that the methods have been determined. The publicity in the provinces and cities will focus on indoor celebration meetings, flag-raising celebrations, and recreational activities. The celebration methods in Beijing will include lantern festivals and celebrity lectures. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Our Representative Urges League of Nations to Pay Attention to the Dangerous Situation in the Far East; Ambitions of Neighboring Countries Not Contained, Seeds of War Lurking; Serious Impact Will Affect Europe

(Geneva) Gu Weijun, the Chinese representative to the League of Nations and ambassador to Paris, delivered a speech at the League of Nations General Assembly this morning, saying that China's political and economic revitalization has made significant progress in the past year. The central government and the southwest have dispelled their suspicions and made peace, and the political unification of the country has been announced. The authorities have taken major steps in improving public health, water conservancy, cooperative development, agriculture, industry, electrical transportation, and the technical aspects of road, rail, and air transportation. The doctor then cited the report of the China Committee of the League of Nations Executive Council as a clear sign of China's progress, and then asked to pay attention to the fact that China's currency and foreign exchange problems have been resolved with remarkable results. Due to the huge difference in the sharp rise and fall of silver prices, China has been troubled by foreign exchange for two years. The plan implemented by the Chinese government in November 1935 was unanimously praised by the country, and it has now produced a stable currency, stable exchange rates, and promoted exports, and the import surplus has been greatly reduced. The doctor once again asked the public to pay attention to the current political situation in the Far East, saying that a certain foreign country's active preparations for war, frequent movements of troops on the border, repeated border disputes, and armed aggression have been expanding day by day, which makes the overall situation potentially dangerous and may break out at any time, and will have serious repercussions affecting Europe. The doctor concluded by stating the recommendations recently announced by China to the League of Nations Secretariat regarding the reform of the League of Nations. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

Strengthening the League of Nations Requires Military Backing

(Geneva) Ambassador Wellington Koo, the representative of our country, delivered a speech at the League of Nations Assembly today, stating that there are two noteworthy aspects of the situation in the Far East: First, China has made significant progress in political and economic development recently. The technical cooperation between the League of Nations and China has also yielded substantial results. Since the implementation of China's new currency system, it has not only consolidated the currency and stabilized foreign exchange but also notably promoted exports and reduced import surpluses. Second, the intensification of military preparations by a certain country is on the verge of erupting, which will inevitably have a significant impact on Europe. Koo also described the situation in Europe, stating that countries are engaged in a race of military build-up, creating a precarious situation. Although there is a tendency towards economic recovery, the economic nationalism of various countries seeks self-sufficiency, increasing various obstacles to international trade. The general trend will continue to hinder the development of trade. Furthermore, the faith in treaties has suffered a major shock, and the psychological respect for international obligations has also been severely undermined. The collective peace system and security guarantees contained in the League of Nations Covenant have not been fully implemented, and even when implemented, they have not achieved the desired results. The problem lies in the slow and incomplete implementation, which often obscures the principles of law and justice for temporary convenience. History is full of precedents of sacrificing principles for temporary convenience, ultimately leading to increased international disputes. The situation in the Far East four years ago is about to be replayed in Europe today. China's faith in the League of Nations Covenant has not changed and firmly believes that the League of Nations is the only mechanism for handling international disputes to achieve peaceful purposes. The reason why the actions of the League of Nations are not fully effective lies not in the imperfection of the Covenant but in the inadequacy of its implementation policies and methods. Therefore, at the invitation of the Executive Yuan, China has drafted a plan to strengthen the important functions of the League of Nations. The various methods stipulated in Article 16 of the Covenant should be regarded as including the methods or actions that the League of Nations is authorized to take under Articles 10 and 11, and should not be excluded. The Chinese government also believes that for the actions of the League of Nations to be effective, it is necessary to make them swift. And during emergencies, swift action requires sufficient preparation in advance. As for the member states using military force to back the League of Nations, the Chinese government firmly believes that the sanctions methods stipulated in Article 16 should also have military force in reserve to produce rapid results. Koo concluded by stating that China hopes to reconvene the disarmament conference and convene an international economic conference to study the economic problems of various countries. China will strive to optimistically contribute to world peace based on collective security. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 29th)

Russian Representative's Speech Advocates for Collective Security, Refutes Hitler's Anti-Russian Remarks, Three Non-Permanent Council Members Elected

(Geneva) The League of Nations General Assembly convened this afternoon and immediately elected three non-permanent members of the Executive Council. The elected countries were Bolivia, New Zealand, and Sweden. Bolivia succeeds Argentina, New Zealand succeeds Australia, and Sweden succeeds Denmark. After the election, the General Assembly continued the general political debate. Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov delivered a speech, exploring the issue of revising the League of Nations Covenant in detail, stating, "Today, some powerful countries have shown obvious signs of aggression, while most countries have not yet realized this aggression.

(Nanjing) Nanjing's agricultural, industrial, and commercial groups are celebrating the birthday of Chairman Chiang. The second preparatory meeting will be held tomorrow. The principles of celebration are: 1. To build a memorial tower in the city center to celebrate Chairman Chiang's birthday. 2. To publish publications to honor his achievements. 3. To hold a celebration ceremony at the Lixingshe. The entire business community of the city will hang flags and light lanterns to celebrate. The location of the memorial tower is suitable in Xinjiekou, but various circles have already designated the site for the statue of Sun Yat-sen, so it will be necessary to conduct a re-examination or select a suitable location on Zhongzheng Road, or in Xuanwu Lake. The expenses will be automatically shared by all circles, or assigned by rank. (Special dispatch on the 29th) The danger is truly regrettable. However, some countries also recognize the necessity of common defense and sincerely believe in upholding the collective security system. If such countries only stop at issuing verbal official statements, while the aggressive countries base their policies on material advantages, it is appropriate that they will be defeated. France's proposal to convene a disarmament conference is sincerely supported by the Soviet Union. However, some countries believe that the League of Nations must become universal to include major countries. If the organization of the League of Nations is not universal, there is no need to do anything. The Soviet Union cannot agree with this view. Since Article 10 of the League of Nations Covenant clearly stipulates that each member state should respect and protect the territorial integrity and political independence of other members, it is natural that those who aim to conquer the territory of other countries, the countries they rule, will not be willing to cooperate with the League of Nations. Now, to revise the League of Nations Covenant to satisfy these countries, it would be better to say that it is to seek the universality of the League of Nations than to say that it is to abolish the basic principles of the League of Nations." Litvinov then advocated that the issue of implementing the principles of the League of Nations Covenant should be submitted to the First Committee (i.e., the Legal and Regulatory Committee) for discussion.

After Litvinov's speech, Danish representative Munch followed with a speech, also opposing the revision of the Covenant but advocating the establishment of a special committee to find ways to improve the mediation procedures for international disputes. The General Assembly adjourned at 6:30 p.m. (Havas dispatch on the 28th)

(Geneva) Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov, at the League of Nations General Assembly today, vehemently refuted the recent remarks made by German leader Hitler at the Nuremberg National Socialist Party Congress, which strongly criticized the Soviet Union, in very sharp terms. The gist of his remarks was that the leader of a country who has listed the expansion of foreign territories that he wants to seize cannot sincerely accept the provisions of Article 10 of the League of Nations Covenant (i.e., the maintenance of the territorial integrity and current political independence of each member state). Moreover, a country that promotes a regional war as legitimate cannot be reconciled with Article 16 of the Covenant (i.e., the provisions on sanctions). Aggressors who base their policies on seizing power through brutal force can only be subdued by combining the relative strength of various countries. The united power of all peace-loving countries in the world must exceed any alliance of aggressors. In today's world, to avoid world war and force aggressors to join the common system of collective security, the joint action of the aforementioned peace-loving countries is indispensable. Litvinov also said, "We do not object to attempts to conclude agreements with the most aggressive countries in the world, but if they manipulate the content of the agreements or offer benefits to induce them to join the negotiations, we cannot agree to that." (Reuters dispatch on the 28th)

Canada Abides by Covenant Principles, Supports Separation from the Treaty of Versailles, Decision to Participate in War Depends on Circumstances

(Geneva) Canadian Prime Minister Mackenzie King stated today at the League of Nations General Assembly regarding Canada's attitude towards participating in possible wars that any decision by Canada to participate in war must be determined by the Canadian Parliament based on all existing circumstances. King then discussed the League of Nations Covenant, detailing the historical position of the Canadian government on this issue, stating that this does not mean that the Canadian people are in no way prepared to participate in actions to resist aggressors, but the natural obligation to use force cannot be made a practical political argument. Canada reaffirms its adherence to the basic principles of the Covenant, but believes that formal amendments to the Covenant are now impossible or unnecessary. Canada supports the separation of the Covenant from the Treaty of Versailles. However, if the League of Nations is to fulfill its duties, it must restore trust and goodwill between European countries. Therefore, the first step of consultation should embrace the goal of attracting countries that have not joined the League of Nations to ultimately succeed in achieving universal membership. (Reuters dispatch on the 29th)

Japan Reforms Administrative Agencies, Military Proposes Concrete Plan

(Tokyo) Minister of the Army Terauchi submitted a written opinion to Prime Minister Hirota on the 21st regarding the Army's views on administrative reform. The contents are roughly as follows:

(1) Establish a comprehensive control mechanism to implement national policies and reform the Cabinet Investigation and other agencies. (2) Establish a minister without portfolio who concurrently serves as the head of the comprehensive agency. (3) Merge the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Colonial Affairs into the Ministry of Foreign Policy, and establish a new Department of Foreign Affairs and a Department of Colonial Affairs. (4) Merge the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry and the Ministry of Commerce and Industry into the Ministry of Industry, and establish a new Department of Agriculture and Forestry and a Department of Commerce and Industry. (5) Merge the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Communications into the Ministry of Transportation, and establish a new Department of Railways, a Department of Communications, and a Department of Aviation. (6) Transfer the affairs of the Civil Engineering Bureau under the Ministry of the Interior to the Ministry of Transportation, and transfer the affairs of the Shrine Bureau to the Ministry of Education. (7) Through the integration of the above ministries, realize the organic combination of administrative affairs and implement seven major national policies: expanding health facilities, economic revitalization of agricultural, mountainous, and fishing villages, promoting small and medium-sized commercial and industrial enterprises, controlling electricity, achieving self-sufficiency in liquid fuels and iron and steel, controlling trade, developing aviation and maritime transportation, and developing overseas Japanese residents. This plan should be implemented starting next year. (Allied News dispatch on the 29th)

Japan Filled With Wartime Atmosphere, Telegraph Bureau Abnormally Tense

(Tokyo) Since the Shanghai Incident, due to the intense attitude of the Army and Navy authorities, the whole country has been filled with a wartime atmosphere. In addition to military aspects, telecommunications and transportation have also shown a degree of tension unseen in four years. According to investigations, the Osaka Central Telegraph Bureau normally sends and receives an average of about 90 telegraphs to and from China daily. Recently, due to the urgency of Sino-Japanese diplomacy, the sending and receiving have been very tense. On the 21st, 111 telegraphs were received, and on the 22nd and 23rd, about 100 telegraphs were received. Between 94 and 97 telegraphs were also sent, and they were all military telegraphs. This shows a glimpse of the internal tension of the Japanese authorities. (China United Press dispatch on the 29th)

Japanese Foreign Minister Decides to Strengthen the Lineup of Foreign Investment in China, Foreign, Army, and Navy Unite as One, Aiming to Achieve Established Policy

(Tokyo) Japanese Foreign Minister Hachiro Arita, Minister of the Army Sugiyama Hajime, and Minister of the Navy Osami Nagano, in view of the increasingly tense Sino-Japanese situation, in addition to actively deploying military forces, also plan to strengthen the diplomatic lineup for the emergency period, so that the three parties can work together as one to achieve their so-called established policy. The specific plan to strengthen the diplomatic lineup has been agreed upon by the three ministers and its contents are as follows and will be implemented soon. (1) Increase the number of special personnel at the Embassy in China. (2) Strengthen the organization of the Consulates General in Shanghai, Hankou, Nanjing, Tianjin, Chengdu, and Guangdong, and expand the information department. (3) Strengthen the Consulate in Zhangjiakou and expand the special service organization. (4) Establish an office of the Embassy in Taiyuan. (5) Establish a new Consulate in Suiyuan. (6) Establish offices of the Consulate General in Datong and Baotou. (7) Increase the number of special work personnel stationed in Bai Lingmiao, Prince De's Palace, Ningxia, Lanzhou, and other places. (8) Increase the number of students studying to investigate the situation in Mongolia, Xinjiang, Tibet, and Qinghai. (China United Press dispatch on the 29th)

Summary of the French New Currency Bill

(Paris) The entire New Currency Bill, consisting of 25 articles, was recently passed by the Chamber of Deputies with 350 votes against 231. Articles 14 and 15, which are the amendments proposed by the left-wing parties regarding wage issues, were first passed by an overwhelming majority of 355 votes against 199. The main points of each article are listed below:

Article 1: The Currency Law of June 25, 1928, which stipulates the gold content of the franc (0.9 parts gold, 0.0655 grams), is repealed.

Article 2: The gold content of the franc will be determined by the government by order, but the gold content shall not be less than 0.043 grams or more than 0.049 grams. The amendment proposed by the right-wing parties in this case, which advocated that the gold content of the franc should be determined by the Chamber of Deputies, has been rejected by the Chamber.

Article 3: Establish an exchange equalization fund.

Article 4: The agreement previously signed by the government and the Bank of France on the 25th of this month, which concerns the revaluation of the bank's gold reserves, is approved.

Article 5: The value of foreign currencies held by the Bank of France will also be revalued.

Article 6: Various international payment obligations that were agreed to be paid in gold coins before the implementation of the new currency are not bound by this law.

Article 7: The value of gold coins and foreign currencies held by issuing banks in various territories should also be revalued.

Article 8: The transaction of gold coins shall not be conducted without the special permission of the Bank of France.

Article 9: Various commercial debts calculated in gold or foreign currencies shall be temporarily suspended. After the passage of this article, Finance Minister Olivar immediately declared that it was rumored that on the 25th of this month, when the government adopted various new currency measures, many people had purchased foreign exchange and sent it to the United Kingdom, and the government would conduct an investigation to find out the truth.

Article 10: All gold coins and gold bars owned by the public shall be nationalized.

Article 11: Anyone who violates the provisions of Article 10 shall be punished.

Article 12: Various punishment measures.

Article 13: The exact number of all foreign exchange transactions, whether futures or spot, completed between September 20 and 26 shall be reported to the Ministry of Finance.

Articles 14 and 15: That is, the amendments concerning wage issues, stipulating that Congress authorizes the government to either prohibit the deliberate raising of prices or use other methods to maintain the domestic purchasing power of the franc and avoid losses to the salaried class.

Article 16: The pensions of veterans should be increased.

Article 17: Various methods to increase pensions.

Article 18: The rights enjoyed by the elderly retirees should be protected.

Articles 19, 20, and 21: Various protection measures.

Article 22: Those who purchase recently issued small-denomination treasury bills should be compensated.

Article 23: The law on pensions should be revised to simplify it.

Article 24: The import duties on various raw materials and food should be adjusted when necessary.

Article 25: The government should lend 3,000,000,000 francs to the French Land Trust Company to reduce mortgage interest. (Havas dispatch on the 29th)

United States Eliminates Narcotics Smuggling, Sends Secret Agents to Various Places

(Washington) The Ministry of Finance today dispatched more than 2,500 secret agents to various parts of the country to eliminate narcotics and liquor smuggling. The Ministry of Finance then decided to launch this elimination campaign. Since the repeal of Prohibition, the authorities have been more passive about liquor smuggling, but the federal government has suffered huge tax revenue losses. This is also related to the current decision to eliminate smuggling. (National News dispatch on the 28th)

Soviet Union Strengthens Far East Military, Army, Navy, and Air Force Lineups Solemn

(Harbin) According to reliable sources, the Soviet military authorities, believing that Japan is actively expanding its military in Manchuria and that the Soviet Far East territories are greatly threatened, have recently dispatched an additional 10 infantry divisions, 3 science corps, 900 aircraft, and 700 heavy tanks to concentrate in Khabarovsk. At the same time, the Pacific Fleet was dispatched to concentrate in Vladivostok, equipped with 800 aircraft, 200 tanks, 60 submarines, and 15 cruisers to prevent invasion. (China United Press dispatch on the 29th)

France Orders Ban on Gold Exports, Chamber of Deputies Passes Coinage Bill, All-Night Discussion, Noise for Half an Hour, Wage Progressive Clause Deleted, Government Authorized to Prohibit Price Increases

(Paris) The government today ordered that all exports, transshipments, and transactions of cash or gold coins, except those introduced by the Bank of France, are temporarily prohibited. This order will be implemented immediately to prevent any cash from escaping the current situation before the new currency bill is established. (Reuters dispatch on the 29th)

(Paris) The National Bank of France today stipulated that the sale of cash must be at least 5 billion francs per unit. Previously, the minimum unit for the sale of cash was 215,000 francs. (National News dispatch on the 28th)

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies held an all-night meeting, which was suspended for half an hour due to noise, and finally passed the bills on the devaluation of the franc and the nationalization of gold today. The bill, which contains 25 articles, was passed with 350 votes against 221. During the debate, Finance Minister Wally Wahre sincerely stated the importance of the international monetary agreement, calling it a turning point in the history of international relations and a symbol of the end of monetary instability. He continued that France can benefit greatly from the agreement. After years of desolation, the sudden emergence of the new currency law is the beginning of a new era. Many members of the Socialist Party and the Left Party then stood up and cheered in approval. The decision was debated fiercely. At 11 p.m. last night, a certain member of the Radical Socialist Party said that some people would enrich themselves by harming the country, causing an uproar and suspending the meeting for half an hour. A certain member of the Right Party spoke in a sarcastic tone, saying that the Blum franc was not made of gold but of rubber. At the same time, negotiations were carried out behind the scenes, and Prime Minister Blum agreed to cancel the provision in the bill that gradually increased wages and replace it with a clause authorizing the government to prevent price increases. After the Left Party accepted this amendment in principle, the Chamber of Deputies passed the amendment with 335 votes against 199. The Senate convened at 11:45 a.m. this morning and accepted the bill, but then adjourned the meeting until tomorrow, so the bill cannot become law before tomorrow. (Reuters dispatch on the 29th)

Situation of Discussions in the House of Representatives

(Paris) The House of Representatives continued its session after noon, discussing the currency bill. The first speaker was the Radical Socialist Party Representative and former Minister of Finance, Painleve. Painleve stated that attention should be paid to the repercussions that currency devaluation could have on the middle class, and that social order should be maintained at all costs, as this was the only way to encourage French capital that had fled abroad to return to France. Painleve criticized the method of indexing wages to prices, saying that this method would cause prices to continue to rise, and the result would be that currency reform would fail.

Following Painleve, former Minister of Finance Renault gave a speech. Renault has the highest authority on financial issues, so his words attracted much attention. He expressed his strong support for the principle of currency devaluation, but said, "Unfortunately, this move is too late. The Bank of France has already lost 300 billion francs in gold reserves. Currency devaluation has become a global phenomenon. Today, it is extremely difficult to find a country that has not devalued its currency. It is only natural for France to devalue its currency now, but we cannot but blame the government for its previous declarations that it did not want to devalue its currency. However, after the promulgation of the new currency bill, the atmosphere of unrest that has prevailed in the country for the past four months will be completely transformed. However, it is not enough for the government to take this one step. At the same time, it must also economize on government spending and balance the budget in order to succeed. Our country's currency is now on par with the two major industrial and commercial nations of Britain and the United States, which is indeed a good plan. However, in the future, we must find ways to make Britain, the United States, and France live in the same economic climate. Therefore, funds flowing out of the country must be recovered, and a large number of unemployed people must be resettled. All of this cannot be done by the currency devaluation policies of either the left or the right. Moreover, currency devaluation, if done well, will benefit the country and the people. However, if it is not done well, it will inevitably lead to continued devaluation, and the consequences will be unimaginable. The government should now frankly declare to the working class that it acknowledges the failure of past experiments, just as the policy of monetary tightening has failed. If this is the case, the working class will surely understand and trust the government. After all, there is no country in the world that is economically bankrupt and where the working class can be happy. Based on past experience, countries around the world that have adopted currency devaluation policies have generally achieved success. Will France be the only country in the future to fail because of adopting a currency devaluation policy? We dare to ask the government officials this question."

After Renault finished speaking, Minister of Finance Olivol rose to reply. Olivol first stated that after Italy, Britain, and the United States successively devalued their currencies, world prices had fallen to below the level before the Great War. Therefore, production and consumption were not in harmony, which was a major cause of the economic panic. As a result, French finances were extremely difficult. At the beginning of this year, the former cabinet's Minister of Finance, Regnier, had to borrow from London. Moreover, the economic panic was not unique to France, but was suffered by countries all over the world. Therefore, since 1933, countries had repeatedly tried to establish international economic agreements. People all over the world had been eagerly awaiting this kind of international cooperation. After several years, it had finally been achieved recently. As far as the current financial situation in France is concerned, the government's deposits in the Bank of France still amount to a huge sum of 80 billion francs, which shows that the devaluation of the currency is not due to financial difficulties. Olivol continued to emphasize the importance of the joint declaration issued by Britain, the United States, and France on currency agreements, saying, "The French government can now guarantee that after the devaluation of the franc, the exchange rate between the pound sterling and the US dollar will not be affected, and other countries will not impose tariff retaliation policies on France because of the devaluation of the franc. From this, it can be seen that the cooperation between Britain, France, and the United States can be said to be fully achieved. Moreover, the extent of this devaluation of the franc is determined according to the leveling of world prices, so domestic prices will definitely not be affected by it and rise. This is different from the policy of inflation, which can affect domestic prices. France suffered deeply from the scourge of inflation after the Great War, and it was not until 1926 that the late Prime Minister Poincaré devalued the currency and stabilized the exchange rate. However, at that time, he suppressed speculation, reorganized finance, and worked hard, and it was not until after 1928 that he achieved success. Now, the government should also follow the methods at that time, handle things in a practical manner, and definitely not allow speculators to profit from it."

After Olivol finished his speech, the House of Representatives adjourned the meeting and reconvened in the evening. During the adjournment period, the various left-wing parties in the House of Representatives held a meeting and decided to delete the section on indexing wages to prices from the currency bill. The Property Party and the General Confederation of Labor both agreed to delete that section and replace it with another section, which stipulated that "The National Assembly authorizes the government to maintain the purchasing power of the franc within the country, or to prohibit improper price increases, or to use other methods, as determined by the government." After this section was deleted and revised, the currency bill will be passed in the National Assembly more smoothly.

At 9:35 p.m., the House of Representatives continued its session. At first, only a few unimportant members of parliament spoke, criticizing the government's bill. In addition to what Painleve and Renault had said during the day, there was nothing new. Then, right-wing Representative Roland spoke, saying that the guarantees that the government had obtained from Britain and the United States were insufficient, and that the currencies of Britain and the United States were not stable, so they were not reliable. Left-wing Republican Representative Delie was concerned about the repercussions of the currency bill on farmers. At this point, Radical Socialist Representative Redol got up angrily and said, "If so, then let the true masters of France, the 200 wealthy families, pay!" (Note: The 200 wealthy families refer to the 200 major shareholders of the Bank of France.) At this point, the entire venue was in an uproar, and the speaker had no choice but to declare a short recess.

At 11:10 p.m., the House of Representatives continued its session. Communist Representative Duglot spoke, saying, "The Communist Party has not benefited from the devaluation of the franc, but the Communist Party will not oppose it." As of the time of writing, the debate in the House of Representatives had not yet ended. It is estimated that the currency bill will be put to a vote late at night or early in the morning. It is expected that the result of the vote will be passed by a large majority. The number of votes in favor will be about the same as the number of votes that the government has received in the House of Representatives several times since June of this year. (Havas Telegram, 28th)

(Paris) Prime Minister Leon Blum personally mounted the rostrum and delivered a long speech, defending this article and explaining the reasons for the government's current currency and general policies. He said, "Regarding the currency issue, I (the Prime Minister referring to himself) and Minister of Finance Olivol have been under pressure from several parties. What these people are asking is that we should devalue the currency immediately after taking office. The main reason is that the national treasury is currently encountering the most serious difficulties. Once devaluation is implemented, a huge sum of 250 billion francs can be obtained immediately. Minister of Finance and I did not accept this opinion at first, and we continued to work hard to engage in the great cause of economic recovery. Now, although we have no choice but to adopt a new currency policy, I am not ashamed of it. It should be known that US President Roosevelt also found a satisfactory method after experiencing exploration regarding the revival of the country's economy. Moreover, I do not admit that what I have done in the past is wrong."

Spanish Rebels 40 Miles From Capital, Government Denies Moving Capital, Rebels Prepare to Strike

(Lisbon) According to a radio message issued by the Burgos rebels indirectly received here, the army has begun to advance from Toledo towards Madrid. (Reuters Telegram, 29th)

(Gibraltar) Spanish rebel General Tranno broadcast a message from the Seville radio station today, saying that the revolutionary army is now only 41 miles from Madrid. (National Telegram, 28th)

(Lisbon) After occupying Toledo, rebel commander General Franco is currently assembling his troops, preparing to quickly attack Madrid. According to today's guest, "We cannot waste time at the moment. Madrid's resistance is not worth laughing at. Once we set out, we can go straight to the city. We will be invincible and indestructible." According to military authorities, the current plans for both sides to attack and defend the capital are roughly as follows. It is expected that the government army will take Navalgarmino and Irilegas on the Madrid-Talavera road as the main defense, in order to cover the traffic on the important railway from Madrid to Valencia. The rebels plan to concentrate at a certain location near Woliaster Le, 40 miles from Madrid, and prepare to attack the government army within a few days. One critic believes that the rebels' attack on the area is unstoppable, because the soldiers in the army have been fighting for a long time and are equipped with the latest weapons, and the commanding officers are also well-trained. According to one correspondent who accompanied the rebel rescue column to be the first to enter the town, although Toledo had undergone street fighting, the whole city was still intact, except for the north side of the Alcázar Castle, which was slightly damaged. One officer and 20 soldiers were the first to enter the city, followed by a detachment of 30 people. After an exchange of fire, the reinforcements penetrated deep into the center of the city. While the government artillery continued to bombard the castle, the planes of both sides soared in the sky, appearing quite active. The remaining warriors who had been trapped in the Alcázar Castle in Toledo for a long time, at a glance of their comrades, shouted Long Live Spain, raised their rifles high, broke out of the siege, and joined the reinforcements, and this historically famous war came to an end. According to official announcement, as a result of the battle, out of the 1,200 people in the Alcázar Castle, 80 were killed, 500 were injured, and the rest were rescued. (Reuters Telegram, 29th)

(Toledo) The remnants of the government army are currently concentrating near Toledo, in order to strengthen the defenses of Madrid. This morning, four three-engine planes and three fighter planes belonging to the National Army bombed the new positions of the government army, while the artillery fired on the highway from Toledo to Madrid, in order to cover the infantry's preparations for attack. (Havas Telegram, 29th)

(Lisbon) Lisbon Daily's special correspondent in Toledo said that the leaders of the National Army believe that after the fall of Toledo, the fall of Madrid is only a matter of time. It is believed that the first fierce contact will be near the capital. Most of the province of Toledo is a plain and is not suitable for defense. The vanguard of the National Army will not easily take the mountainous road before the capture of the Getafe airfield near the capital. (National Telegram, 29th)

(La Vera) The government army and the rebel army fought fiercely all day today to compete for the entire province of Toledo. The rebel headquarters today officially announced that 80 of the 1,200 soldiers defending the Alcázar Castle were killed and 500 were injured. During the siege, the castle was hit by 6,000 three-inch shells and 4,000 5.9-inch shells. (National Telegram, 28th)

Internal Organization of the Income Tax Affairs Office, Divided into Five Groups with Assigned Responsibilities

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance announced that the second category of income tax on the salaries and remuneration of civil servants and the third category of income tax on the interest income of public bonds and savings deposits will be levied on October 1st. It is currently reorganizing the Central Direct Tax Preparatory Office into an Income Tax Affairs Office, in order to coordinate the collection of income tax. Gao Bingfang and Liang Jingchun will continue to serve as the director and deputy director of the office. The internal organization is planned to be divided into five groups, and the responsibilities of each group have been assigned. The first group is responsible for the income of profit-making enterprises, the second group is responsible for the income of salaries and wages, the third group is responsible for the income of securities deposits, the fourth group is responsible for accounting, and the fifth group is responsible for affairs. The candidates for the group leader are tentatively Ning Encheng, Zhang Hua, Qu Zhaorong, Sun Chaoxuan, and Sun Xiaocun. Other office staff are all transferred from the original Central Direct Tax Preparatory Office and the Central Party Headquarters that handled income donations. The procedures for collecting the two categories of income that will be levied on October 1st are relatively simple, as they are all withheld by various agencies, so they are handled directly by the Income Tax Affairs Office. There is no need to set up collection agencies in various provinces and cities for the time being. Only the Ministry of Finance will first send personnel to contact and guide the withholding in various ways. All income taxes withheld by various agencies from October 1st onwards should be submitted to the local Central Bank or the China Communications Bank and the Postal Remittance Bureau entrusted by the Central Bank for transfer to the national treasury. As for banks and money houses, they will only withhold income tax on interest income on savings deposits that have reached settlement from October 1st onwards. Those that need to be settled at the end of the year should be withheld at the time of settlement declaration. In addition, the income donation collected by the central government will be stopped on the 30th. (Central News Agency Telegram, 29th)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance sent a telegram to the various ministries, departments, committees, provincial and municipal governments, and the national banking and money industry associations on the 29th, stating that from October 1st, they should separately deduct and submit the income of civil servants' salaries and remuneration and the interest income of public bonds and savings deposits in accordance with the Interim Regulations on Income Tax and the Detailed Rules for Implementation to the local Central Bank or its entrusted agency for transfer to the national treasury. In addition, the income donation originally collected by the central government will be discontinued on the 30th. (Central News Agency Telegram, 29th)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Municipal Government has prepared to collect income tax and will start on schedule. The taxes payable by civil servants in various municipal agencies will be withheld when expenses are issued each month. The original income donation collection in the city will be cancelled after income tax is collected. (Special Telegram, 29th)

(Guangzhou) In order to assist the government in implementing income tax, the Guangdong Provincial Party Department has formulated six measures to expand publicity to the public and explain the truth about income tax. (Central News Agency Telegram, 29th)

National Election Headquarters Explains Qualifications for Journalists: President, Editor-in-Chief, and Manager All Considered Journalists

(Nanjing) The National Election Headquarters stated that due to inconsistencies in the organization of journalists' groups in various regions, and in order to facilitate participation in the election, it has, based on the interpretation of the General Office of the National Assembly Election, divided the staff of newspapers and news agencies into three categories: workers' groups, business groups, and freelance professional groups. Those who engage in interviewing, editing, and commenting in newspapers and news agencies should, in all fairness, be classified as freelance professionals. The term "editor" in the interpretation refers generically to those engaged in interviewing, editing, and commenting. Persons such as the president and editor-in-chief should be regarded as journalists. If the newspaper or news agency adopts a management system, the manager, whose position is equivalent to that of the president, should also be regarded as a journalist. Relevant departments are required to comply with these regulations. The Headquarters has recently sent a letter to the Freelance Professional Groups Election Office for notification. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Land Ownership Dispute Cases

(Nanjing) Regarding land ownership dispute cases in various provinces and cities, the Judicial Yuan has clarified that before the promulgation of the "Regulations on the Organization of Land Courts," judicial organs should directly handle such cases without going through mediation procedures. Subsequently, various provinces and cities requested instructions from the Ministry of Interior, believing that this decision by the Judicial Yuan would greatly hinder the progress of land registration. The Ministry of Interior then submitted a report to the Executive Yuan, ordering it to consult with the Ministry of Finance for review, and requesting the Judicial Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Justice to send personnel to participate in the discussion. It was agreed that disputes over land rights arising during the registration process should be handled by the land administration organs within a certain period by ordering them to apply to the judicial organs for handling before the establishment of the land courts. Those who fail to apply within the time limit may be investigated by the land administration organs. Those who disagree with their mediation should still be ordered to apply to the judicial organs for handling. This has been approved by the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Interior has issued instructions to the governments of various provinces and cities for investigation and notification on the 29th. (29th Special Dispatch)

American Sailor Arrested and Sentenced in Berlin: Imprisoned for Three Years for Promoting Communism; United States Awaits Official Report

(Berlin) More than a year ago, an American sailor, Simpson, was arrested in Hamburg on charges of treason and espionage. Today, he has been sentenced to three years in prison by the "People's Court." He has been detained for four months before the verdict, which can be reduced accordingly. At the hearing today, the Nazi prosecutor did not file espionage charges, but only said that Simpson had communist activities in Germany. The evidence was that Simpson had carried communist slogans and pamphlets when he arrived in Hamburg. Simpson said, "I don't know what harm these printed materials have, because the Communist Party can hold open meetings in the United States and can elect its own presidential candidates." At that time, a former member of the German Communist Youth Movement named Rez testified that Simpson had repeatedly delivered communist texts and letters from the American Communist Party to the Hamburg branch of the German Communist Party. Simpson denied this. The court today also appointed a lawyer to defend Simpson, arguing that Simpson did not spread communist texts in Germany, but because the United States has always taken a laissez-faire attitude, the Communist Party is naturally easier to operate in the United States than in Germany. The prosecutor requested a sentence of four years in prison, and the defendant's lawyer argued for a maximum of one year. As a result, a three-year sentence was handed down. (28th Guomin Report)

(Washington) The U.S. State Department told the Associated Press today that it is awaiting the official report from U.S. Consul Kissel in Berlin regarding the trial of the American sailor Simpson, who was sentenced to three years in prison in Germany today on charges of espionage and treason, before it can decide what steps to take. The authorities declined to make a formal statement on the outcome of the trial, but said that Germany attaches great importance to communist activities, and Simpson admitted in court that he had communist activities, so the three-year prison sentence is still considered lenient. (28th Guomin Report)

Japanese Build Airfield by Force in Baotou; County Magistrate's Attempt to Stop Them is Ineffective

Baotou Dispatch: For a year, Japanese aircraft have been quite frequent in their coming and going to Baotou. Recently, they are again planning to fly regularly to transport passengers and goods, and also plan to build an airfield in Baotou. The site has already been surveyed in Bancun, two and a half miles outside the South Gate. The local authorities were not aware of this beforehand. When the Japanese were surveying the site by car a few days ago, they accidentally knocked down a telegraph pole. The Public Security Bureau sent personnel to investigate and only then learned that an airfield was going to be built. The bureau questioned them at the time and expressed opposition, but the Japanese said that the land was ownerless. Currently, the Japanese have entrusted the Fuchang Company in the Tianjin French Concession to hire more than 30 Chinese workers to come to Baotou a few days ago, and have also hired four Japanese workers. According to the Chinese workers, when the company recruited in Tianjin, it stated that they were going to work in Zhangjiakou, but did not state that they were working for the Japanese. After arriving in Zhangjiakou, they said they were going to work in Suiyuan. After arriving in Suiyuan, they said they were going to work in Baotou. When they set off from Tianjin, each Chinese worker received an advance of five yuan from the employer for family expenses, and the daily wage was set at 80 cents. The Chinese workers also said that had they known they were building an airfield for the Japanese, they would never have been hired. The airfield started construction on the 24th of this month. Zhao Zhongrong, the county magistrate of Baotou, negotiated with Hamada, the Japanese official stationed in Baotou, to stop it. According to Hamada, he had already obtained the consent of Chairman Fu Zuoyi of Suiyuan. Zhao then asked Chairman Fu for instructions. Fu not only expressed that he did not know about it, but also ordered Zhao to find a way to stop it. On the morning of the day before, Zhao sent Song Mingqing, the director of the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and Du Xiapu, the director of the Third Branch, and several police officers to negotiate at the airfield. At this time, Hamada and the four Japanese workers had left the airfield and entered the city. The thirty-odd Chinese workers, who understood the greater good, saw that Song and others had come to negotiate, and immediately stated that they were willing to sacrifice their labor and follow Song and others into the city, and were unwilling to work for the Japanese, and asked for a way to send them back to their hometowns. Song and others immediately took them all to the Public Security Bureau and reported to County Magistrate Zhao, so that he could negotiate with Hamada to stop it. However, Hamada had already heard about it, and sent personnel to the Public Security Bureau in the afternoon to negotiate for the handover of the Chinese workers. County Magistrate Zhao handed over all the Chinese workers, and they were still led away by the Japanese. At about 8:00 PM, when it was already late, a Japanese aircraft flew from Suiyuan to Baotou, circled the city once, and landed at the Eurasia Airfield outside the city, presumably to negotiate. However, according to County Magistrate Zhao, he is determined to find a way to stop it.

Jiangsu Provincial Government to Start Digging New Canal Within This Year; Survey Already Completed, Funds Being Planned; Establishing Reclamation Area Management Committee to Improve Cotton Industry

(Zhenjiang Dispatch) The Jiangsu Provincial Standing Committee's problem of developing the Northern Jiangsu Salt Reclamation Area, previously invited people from Shanghai's banking and industrial circles to visit, and also implemented the surveying of the new canal line in the reclamation area. The surveying work has now been completed. After this, the work in the reclamation area will become more specific. Currently, Jiangsu Province is planning to raise funds for the opening of the new canal and for the improvement of the cotton industry. The latest information obtained is summarized as follows:

New Canal Line Survey Completed

In order to prosper Northern Jiangsu, develop the reclamation area, revitalize commerce, and relieve the rural areas, the Jiangsu Provincial Government decided to open a new canal line to the east of the Grand Canal, starting from Nantong and going north to Chenjiagang Port in Guanyun. It also organized a survey team, appointing Xu Nanxou as the team leader, and led technicians to survey the new canal line. After leaving to implement the survey in March of this year, after half a year of effort, the survey has now been completed. Currently, the team is working on design and drawing charts, etc., which can be completed in about one or two months. The problem of opening up can be realized within this year. The cost is about 10 million yuan, which is currently being planned by the provincial government.

Establishment of Reclamation Area Management Committee

In order to develop the reclamation area, the Jiangsu Provincial Government decided to start with improving the cotton industry and opening up cotton fields. Therefore, the Jiangsu Provincial Cotton Production Improvement Office was established in Nantong to handle cotton breeding and other work. On the other hand, it is actively planning to complete the new canal project in order to promote the development of farmland. However, the reclamation area is vast, and it is difficult to achieve development and promotion without concentrating manpower and financial resources. It is now planned to establish a Coastal Reclamation Area Management Committee in the reclamation area, directly under the jurisdiction of the provincial government. In terms of organization, there will be one chairman and one vice-chairman (there is a saying that the candidate for chairman is concurrently held by Director Shen Jian). Under the committee, there will be one secretary and three departments: General Affairs, Reclamation, and Economics, with specialized personnel appointed. This plan is being reviewed by the provincial authorities. It is said that if the Reclamation Design Committee is realized in the future, it will be merged into the Reclamation Department in order to concentrate efforts and coordinate management.

Provincial Government Allocates Funds to Improve Cotton Industry

The cultivated cotton fields in the province's cotton reclamation area have reached more than 13 million mu, and there are more than 6 million mu that have not yet been cultivated. In order to actively develop the cotton industry, the provincial government previously invited the banking industry to inspect and requested as much investment as possible. Currently, this issue is still under negotiation. According to Cao Jikuan, deputy director of the Agricultural Management Committee, the provincial government, in view of the urgent need to develop the cotton industry, has decided to allocate 100,000 yuan first for this year's cotton industry improvement. The detailed distribution method has been ordered to be drafted by the Improvement Office. The improvement methods will start with investigation and production registration. As the cotton crop matures, it has been harvested everywhere. This year's harvest is still good. The Agricultural Management Committee will soon hold registration matters to engage in the first step of improvement.

Jiangsu Provincial Cotton Industry Improvement Policy

The various points regarding the opening of the reclamation area and the improvement of the cotton industry are as described above. The policy for improving the cotton industry is as follows: (1) Improve cotton seeds and improve the cotton industry in order to improve quality and increase production. Therefore, for Chinese cotton, attention should be paid to improving the lint quality, increasing the ginning percentage, and purifying the species. For American cotton, attention should be paid to maintaining its original improved characteristics, accelerating the maturation period, and increasing its salt resistance and boll resistance to rain. (2) Pest prevention and control. There are many types of cotton insects, and their harmful conditions vary with seasons, regions, varieties, and cultivation methods. Efforts should be made to prevent and control them in order to reduce cotton farmers' losses. (3) Improve saline land. The area of saline reclamation in northern Jiangsu is very large, but because the salt content is too high, it is not suitable for crop growth, and it has become wasteland. It is planned to study improvement so that cotton crops can grow appropriately to increase soil production. (4) Eliminate accumulated habits. Chinese cotton farmers have the bad habit of adding water and adulterating cotton, and cotton merchants have the malpractice of suppressing and manipulating cotton prices, so that the quality of cotton cannot be improved. Honest cotton farmers also follow suit because the high-quality cotton they produce cannot get a fair price. These accumulated habits must be eliminated in order to improve.

Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau's Recent Progress: Hangzhou Installs Long-Distance Amplifiers; Selectively Installs Terminal Amplifiers; Province Opens Up Communication with Beijing and Shanghai

Zhejiang Province's telephone business has always been known for its development, especially the long-distance telephone item. After the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau's intention to operate, the completeness of the telecommunications network is the crown of all provinces in the country. Previously, the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau, with the province's long-distance telephones spread throughout the cities and towns, and has been in contact with Jiangsu, Jiangxi, Fujian provinces, communication locations are increasing day by day, and the mileage of the line is also increasing day by day. In order to improve the clarity of long-distance calls, it has actively planned to install telephone amplifiers in various important bureaus to increase the volume of long-distance transmission. It is now known that the amplifier in the Hangzhou No. 1 Bureau is a cord circuit 23 type amplifier, which can be 20 times more effective, has been installed first, and the farthest Yongjia and other places in the province have been tested with Nanjing, Shanghai and other places. The result of the transmission is quite clear, and it will be enabled immediately. At the same time, the bureau selectively installs terminal amplifiers next to long-distance telephones in important bureaus and the bureau's retail outlets in the Hangzhou National Products Exhibition Hall, etc., so that the volume transmitted from long distances can be amplified 12 to 20 times. It is also known that the bureau has decided to open up telephone communication with Nanjing, Shanghai and other places in Jiangsu Province from October 1. All telephones from Beijing, Shanghai and other places to the southeast of the province are required to be temporarily connected through the Hangzhou amplifier. In the future, the volume of calls will definitely be clear.

Songjiang: Farmers in Hutang Township Robbed

Su Bingsheng's family, a farmer in Hutang Township, Fifth Bao, Eighth Jia, Eighth District, Punan, was attacked by more than ten bandits at about 11:00 PM on the 24th. They all spoke in a local dialect and carried rifles, wooden sticks, and other weapons. They broke the kitchen window and entered to rob. Later, they went to the adjacent third household, Su Yinxing's family, and rummaged through boxes and chests in each room. When the owner, Su Yinxing, resisted slightly, he was hit on the head. After two hours, they fled with the stolen goods. The owners dared not report the incident for fear of the bandits taking revenge. Later, it was learned by the Ninth Sub-Garrison, which sent police to investigate. Only then did they learn that the stolen clothes and silver dollars were worth nearly 100 yuan. The bureau has been notified to order its subordinates to assist in the arrest.

The office of the Third District Commissioner's Office and Security Command, the newly built People's Education Center in the Confucius Temple, is too small and insufficient for office work. After reporting to the provincial government for approval, it will all move into the old Viceroy's Yamen for office work tomorrow (30th).

Kunshan: Early Rice Rent Paid in Advance

The terrain of this county is low-lying, especially in the northwest. Recently, due to frequent floods and insect plagues, rice is often transplanted early. The early rice has now been harvested, and the late rice is about to be harvested. However, according to the long-standing custom, rent is not collected until after the Frost's Descent Festival. The tenant farmers have already consumed all the blood and sweat they have earned in gambling. When the landlords propose to collect, they are often unable to pay. The educational bureau and other agencies, and more than 20 landlords including Wu Meinong, jointly presented a petition to County Magistrate Peng, requesting that he find a way to improve the situation and collect rent earlier. It is now learned that it has been stipulated that tenant farmers who plant early rice will start to pay rent ten days after the Autumn Equinox.

Strange Visitor Suddenly Appears at Central School

Although he was stopped by the gatekeeper, he ignored it and entered the school, took out a camera, and took pictures of the students. He was later encountered in front of Ma'anshan. When he was taken to the bureau for questioning, he claimed to be surnamed Dong and was from Liaoning.

Changshu: Timetable Change for Xihu Bus

The Xihu Long-Distance Bus Company has recently changed its bus schedule in order to facilitate passengers due to the gradual shortening of the sundial. The main ones are to delay the first bus in the morning to 7:00 AM and advance the last bus in the afternoon to 5:05 PM. The bus to Shanghai will be moved even earlier to 3:35 PM.

Suzhou: Autumn Harvest Colors in Various Townships

This year's early rice in various townships has been a bumper harvest. However, with the exception of the southwest and northwest townships, which can be harvested by more than 90%, the eastern townships such as Chefang, Xietang, Tianjing, and Guoxiang are slightly inferior in harvest due to the impact of wind and insect damage. In the Tianjing and Xuanzhu townships in the Weiting area, the harvest is only about half due to wind, insects, and other factors. According to recent observations, the average autumn harvest in this county is about 70-80%, and at most 90%.

Another Case of Accidental Death

The family of Jia Chang Jiang Yunbin in the sixth Bao, second Jia, and third household of Chefang Guanpu Township had an elderly mother, Zhao, a wife, Zhou, and a five-year-old girl named Wu Bao. It will not be difficult to get through the Mid-Autumn Festival safely. Other industries such as rice, beans, miscellaneous grains, silk cloth, southern goods, mountain goods, and department stores also have the hope of making a profit.

Bengbu: Disputes Arise from Buying Wheat

This year's bumper harvest in northern Anhui has not been seen in many years. Flour mills from north and south have sent people to gather in Bengbu to set up shops to buy wheat. Since the noon season, the wheat market has been quite active. Grain shops act as agents to purchase on behalf of customers, charging a commission of 8 cents per stone. Grain shops with activity compete to be bought by flour mills to make profits. Under the circumstances of soliciting and attracting customers, unexpected disputes have occurred. Recently, the person in charge of the Bengbu wheat shop of Yicheng Flour Mill in Zhenjiang suddenly announced that after the wheat purchased by the factory in Bengbu this year was transported to the factory, it was found that there were abuses such as mixing in dampness, mixing in hair, and short weighing, and wrote to the grain industry agencies, requesting the elimination of bad elements among the grain-selling boat households and staff members. The members of the Grain Industry Association and the Salt and Grain Staff Vocational Union here were in an uproar when they saw this, believing that the shop deliberately damaged its reputation, and expressed their indignation, sending letters to the Yicheng General Factory one after another, and planned to negotiate with the shop to resolve it according to law.

The Japanese Aiming for Financial Gains in the Great Barrier Reef

— Written by Nettie Palmer of Australia, translated by Bu Ren

Recently, the Australian government has felt severely uneasy because Japanese ships often appear in the waters of northern Australia, and Japanese people often land on the coasts of the Australian continent, which no one has ever cared about. Lighthouse keepers reported such repeated intrusions by the Japanese, and holiday travelers camping in quiet harbors also witnessed large numbers of Japanese landing to search for food.

Of course, it is natural for those who regularly catch abalone and sea cucumber to see this group of Japanese who have come from across the sea as formidable rivals for their business; they demand that the government find ways to stop them.

The Japanese also come to collect abalone. Their arrival is bound to cause a rather difficult international dispute. The crux of the problem lies in the Great Barrier Reef. The Great Barrier Reef is a mixture of islands, sand beaches, and coral reefs, surrounding the coast of Queensland, one of the states of the Commonwealth of Australia, about 1,200 miles long, forming a breakwater on the Pacific coast. The distance between the Great Barrier Reef and the mainland coast varies, some reaching twenty miles, some reaching fifty miles. Enclosed within this is a calm sea, which is usually considered Australian territorial waters.

However, this traditional ownership has become a problem due to the intrusion of the Japanese. Because the Japanese have long envied the abundance and value of marine products in the waters of the Great Barrier Reef, they have now begun to invade.

For example, abalone shells are produced here. Every year, 1.5 million pounds of abalone shells are exported from the Great Barrier Reef, most of which are shipped to Japan. This is a coarse and easily polished shell. Because the Japanese obtain this cheap raw material, and because Japanese families usually have their own shell grinding machines, the Japanese have defeated Europeans and Americans, who use expensive pearl shells as raw materials for mother-of-pearl, in the mother-of-pearl button market.

The most important purpose of the Japanese invasion of the Great Barrier Reef is to plunder the raw material for making buttons – the abalone shell. Their usual method of intrusion is to moor the mother ship on the outer shore of the Great Barrier Reef and steer small boats into the inner sea through narrow streams.

My husband and I have been camping on a small island in the Great Barrier Reef for almost a year, so I understand very well the difficulties of managing these waters and the attitude of the local boatmen towards intruders from across the sea. The small island where we live is one of the ring-shaped coral islands along the Great Barrier Reef.

This small island is purely composed of coral, about forty acres in area, but there are also lush jungles on the island. The island is surrounded by a shallow swamp, surrounded by irregularly shaped reefs, with rugged reef surfaces exposed at low tide, on which we sometimes walk for several miles. This is an ideal lookout point, where we can leisurely observe the structure of the Great Barrier Reef and become familiar with the aquatic life of the Great Barrier Reef residents.

For newcomers, the Great Barrier Reef is indeed a miracle. At first, we imagined that the Great Barrier Reef was just a continuous coral wall leaning against the coast like a fortress. After on-the-spot observation, we realized that it was a complex fortress composed of many coral bodies with different degrees of development, with coral reefs exposed at high tide, coral reefs completely above the water surface, old reefs covered with sand and grass, and beach reefs that are the same as usual and grow beautiful trees. We saw all of this in just a short day's voyage.

The people we saw were mostly fishermen from the mainland and boatmen living on the island. In the last fifty years, the navigation industry in the waters of the Great Barrier Reef has made considerable progress. The headquarters of this business is located on Thursday Island in the Torres Strait, where a large number of shallow-water fishing boats are manufactured and sold. These fishing boats are mostly owned by Australians, operated by natives, and the captains are mostly Japanese.

Every year in March, at the end of the rainy cyclone season, these fishing boats depart from the south, gradually moving north, carried by the trade winds. When they reach a suitable location, they anchor for about a week, sending small boats to collect marine products such as abalone, sea cucumber, and pearl shells. Their actions are supervised by the Australian government: the coral reef itself is not allowed to be damaged in the slightest, and the capture of shells less than two and a half inches in diameter is also prohibited. This supervision is quite easy because the marine products collected by these fishing boats must pass through Thursday Island, where they are loaded and exported.

In addition to industrial value, the Great Barrier Reef is a place where indigenous people – whether living on the mainland or on the island – make a living. Diving and collecting seems to be a natural talent for them, just like primitive people living by hunting.

I still remember the first time I saw a group of boatmen coming to our island. Their small boat happened to be parked outside the reef.

"Who owns your boat!" I asked, my eyes fixed on the small boat.

One of them proudly shook his head.

"Our boat is not owned by anyone else, it is owned by ourselves."

Later I learned that on their island – Badu Island – the Queensland government has implemented a cooperative system in recent years, that is: the government provides loans to the natives, asking them to prepare their own boats, and the marine products collected are purchased by the government. This system seems to be quite effective, because the living standards of those natives have improved a lot compared to the past.

The boatmen of the Great Barrier Reef are really a lovely group of people! They are mostly of mixed race. They come from the islands in the Torres Strait (which was originally a place of contact between different ethnic groups), and from their appearance we can guess that their ancestors were Malays, Polynesians, Melanesians, and aborigines of the Australian continent. Regardless of their origin, they generally love the Great Barrier Reef and are proud to be residents of the Great Barrier Reef. From their singing, we understand their proud feelings. When they go ashore for recreation, it is not difficult to ask them to sing in our tent.

They usually sing simple and repetitive lyrical songs, some of which are composed by themselves, and some of which imitate tunes from other places. These lyrics mostly describe their own life at sea and the storms and other dangers they encounter. They also often hold banquets, singing and dancing together, forming a majestic and funny group performance.

Gradually, the Great Barrier Reef waters, a paradise, has begun to be noticed by people other than those who make a living locally. Every sunny winter, travelers from the cold south often come here to travel; in the palm groves, houses have been built to accommodate tourists.

Not many years ago, a British natural science research expedition led by Dr. C.M. Yonge came to Low Woody Island, about forty miles north of our small island; they came to investigate the nature of marine plankton (food for whales) and study coral problems.

According to recent reports, another scientific research expedition will come again. There are originally many questions about coral growth, and the islands of the Great Barrier Reef are nothing less than a natural laboratory for studying these questions.

However, in addition to being related to scientific issues, the Great Barrier Reef is also a main body of political issues that are bound to cause disputes. Should the waters between the Great Barrier Reef and the mainland be considered Australian territory? Is the intrusion of the Japanese a kind of theft? In the near future, these questions will be presented to the world.

Income Tax to be Implemented Tomorrow, Banking and Money Industries Prepared to Implement, Money Industry Notifies Members to Convene a General Meeting, Municipal Chamber of Commerce Prints and Distributes Regulations and Detailed Rules

After the income tax on interest from securities deposits is approved and implemented tomorrow, the Banking Association prepares all procedures, the Money Industry Association notifies the convening of a meeting, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce prints and distributes income tax regulations and detailed rules. The details are recorded as follows:

Banking Preparations

After the temporary member representative meeting of the Banking Association decided to comply with the order of the Ministry of Finance and implement the income tax, it decided to wait for the Central Direct Tax Preparation Office to issue the various income tax forms and instructions before notifying the member banks to comply. As for the opinions proposed by the Banking Association, which are divided into two categories: explanation and revision, they have been submitted to the member banks for research. After the opinions obtained from the research are returned to the meeting, they will be compiled and contributed to the Ministry of Finance for adoption.

Money Industry Meeting

Since the Money Industry Association decided to organize an income tax research committee, the candidates for the committee members (six people have been nominated by the Autumn Managers Meeting and the Executive Committee Meeting, and the remaining three will be nominated by the members general meeting on October 2. The notice has been issued to convene a members general meeting. The notice states: Respectfully, October 2 is the date of the 12th members representative general meeting of the third session of this association. I hope that your representative will come to this association at 2 pm on that day to attend and discuss, and jointly plan the progress. I pray for your happiness. Shanghai Money Industry Association Executive Committee.

Chamber of Commerce Prints and Distributes

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has determined that the income tax on salaries and interest will be levied from October 1. It has printed many copies of the regulations and implementation rules for the business community to consult. The association specially notified all associations in the city yesterday that if they need any, they can contact the association's affairs section at any time. Each copy will be charged a cost of 3 cents.

Liang Goes to Beijing

According to the Central News Agency, the Banking Association believes that the regulations and implementation rules for the securities and deposit interest income tax organized by the Ministry of Finance do not have specific provisions. Therefore, the Banking Association has studied and formulated various points. After discussion at the temporary members general meeting the day before, it was decided to submit them to the member banks for research, and another meeting will be convened in the near future to discuss them. As of last night, no opinions have been submitted to the association. Today happens to be the Mid-Autumn Festival, and all banks are closed. Therefore, this matter will not be able to be discussed until the first day of next month at the earliest. It is also planned to send representatives to the Ministry of Finance to make representations. However, the association has informed the member banks to comply with the Ministry of Finances order to start operations on the first day, and in fact, it will not be possible to forward it to branches in various places for unified handling until the method is determined and various forms are issued. The income tax that should be deducted before the start of operations will be deducted by each bank, but the banks will not be responsible for those that have already been paid out. It is also learned that the Central Direct Tax Office will be established in Beijing on the first day, and responsible persons will be assigned to each province and city. The Shanghai Office will be headed by Deputy Director Liang Jingchun. After Liang went to Beijing the night before to ask for instructions, he immediately took the forms and tax collection instructions to Shanghai.
