Shanghai's Anti-Smoking Campaign Enters a New Stage, Great Results Achieved in the Chinese Area, Concessions Still Awaiting Continued Negotiations

According to the Central News Agency, the registration of smokers in Shanghai has ended, and Ma Liang, the commissioner sent by the central government to Shanghai to handle registration and reporting, is about to leave Shanghai and return to Beijing to report on his mission. Therefore, the anti-smoking affairs in Shanghai will now enter a new stage. A reporter from the Central News Agency specially visited Commissioner Ma to inquire about the past registration of smokers and future anti-smoking measures. The information learned is recorded as follows:

Past Smoker Registration

Commissioner Ma first stated the past smoker registration situation, briefly saying that during the past reporting period, those who had already registered and obtained licenses before the period and whose licenses had expired and went to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to renew their licenses totaled more than 19,000 people. During the reporting period, more than 24,000 people applied for supplementary registration. More than 11,000 people had already quit smoking, and more than 1,000 people had left the city or died. This is the situation obtained after several months of investigation.

Reporting Work for Three Months

Since the establishment of the Commissioner's Office in early May, after nearly a month of preparation work and a month of closing work, the actual reporting work was only three months. Fortunately, the local authorities and leaders provided timely assistance, so great results have been achieved in the Chinese area. Even in the concessions, considerable results have been obtained. Now that the closure of the office has been completed, Ma will leave Shanghai within days to visit General Supervisor Jiang in Beijing to report on the registration of smokers in Shanghai. Ma expressed his gratitude to the local leaders in Shanghai for their enthusiastic assistance in handling the anti-smoking policy, and also expressed his gratitude to the news media for promoting the government's purpose of anti-smoking at any time.

Concession Anti-Smoking Issues

Commissioner Ma reiterated the past negotiations on anti-smoking in the concessions in Shanghai, briefly saying that Shanghai is a place where Chinese and foreigners live together, so it is difficult to handle anti-smoking affairs. In the Chinese area, the anti-smoking policy is carried out in accordance with central laws and regulations, but because it is difficult to promote in the concessions, the anti-smoking policy in Shanghai is greatly affected. Therefore, I am very concerned about this matter. The city had drafted opinions and submitted them to the headquarters, requesting negotiations with the consular corps. The headquarters immediately consulted the Executive Yuan and handed it over to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for handling. However, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs believed that diplomatic procedures were time-consuming and requested the local government to directly negotiate with the consular corps. Therefore, the headquarters ordered me to reply, and I had repeatedly consulted with Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government. Secretary-General Yu had begun to exchange opinions with the concession authorities, and local leaders in Shanghai, such as Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, and Yu Qiaqing, had also made suggestions to the concession authorities. Initially, the concession authorities did not fully understand China's anti-smoking policy. After repeated statements from all parties about the determination of the Chinese government to ban smoking, and explaining the steps to carry out anti-smoking, they have now been able to fully understand it. However, due to procedural issues, future consultations should be continued to determine specific measures that can be taken in the same way as in the Chinese area to promote the anti-smoking campaign. Then, the anti-smoking affairs in Shanghai will be able to achieve even greater results in the future.

More Than 10,000 People Quit Smoking

Commissioner Ma finally talked about the future anti-smoking policy, saying that there are a large number of smokers in Shanghai. More than 10,000 people have already quit smoking, and the anti-smoking hospitals in Shanghai are still continuing to actively handle the anti-smoking work. In the current situation, about 1,000 people can quit smoking every month. However, if smokers who have already quit smoking are not properly handled, there is a risk of relapse. Therefore, I believe that efforts should be made to establish smoker factories or other production organizations. One is to enable the smokers who have quit smoking to be managed and supervised in an orderly manner, and the other is to enable them to engage in production. Moreover, if the concessions in Shanghai can proceed in accordance with Chinese laws and regulations, the anti-smoking policy will be less complicated. Furthermore, all negotiations are still ongoing, so the headquarters will send personnel to the provinces and cities to permanently preside over the anti-smoking policy. Awaiting the headquarters research, I will report the situation in Shanghai after going to Beijing, and will attend the National Anti-Smoking Conference. At this conference, the future anti-smoking affairs will be discussed, and General Supervisor Chen will decide.

Three Banks Transport Cash to Guangdong to Replenish Fractional Currency Reserves, National Monetary Unification Can Be Completed From Now On, Impact of Three-Country Currency Agreement on Exchange Rate Reduced

According to the Central News Agency, there have been rumors that the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications are transporting cash to Guangdong. The reporter specially visited the Central Bank to meet with the responsible officials to inquire about the truth. It is said that the monetary system of Guangdong Province has been reorganized by the central government. The total amount of fractional currency previously issued in the province was more than 249 million yuan. The shortage of the 60% cash reserve was more than 17%. The Ministry of Finance is now borrowing the full amount from the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, and will continue to transport it to Guangdong to replenish it. After this, the fractional currency reserves of Guangdong Province have been replenished in accordance with the law. The provinces financial economy must trend toward improvement, and the promotion of legal tender must increase. The three banks are aware of this and plan to continue to transport cash to increase the issuance reserves. During the conversation, the reporter asked about the currency agreement between the United Kingdom, the United States, and France. The responsible official replied that the United Kingdom, France, and the United States have entered into a currency agreement to strengthen the monetary systems of the European and American powers, to make prices tend to a consistent balance, and to promote economic cooperation. From now on, the ratio between the British and American gold and the French franc will be stable. Chinas legal tender is closely related to foreign exchange, and the exchange rate between the United Kingdom and the United States is particularly important. Now that the currencies of the three countries have been agreed upon, the exchange rate of legal tender should be more stable, and the impact of exchange rate changes will be reduced.

The society has reached its 13th annual meeting since its establishment. We now have over 700 members, with over 300 permanent members, bringing together talent from the political, business, and academic fields, which is truly a great phenomenon. Annual meetings held in various places are deeply welcomed, and everyone attaches great importance to them. This annual meeting has many special aspects, including a debate in addition to the reading of papers. However, due to time constraints, I was unable to attend as much as I would have liked. At the opening ceremony of the annual meeting the day before yesterday, Minister Kong mentioned that the economic recovery of the United States, while relying on the proper leadership of the government, ultimately benefited from the influence of economists. China's current economic situation has indeed reached a critical juncture, and how to find a solution is a responsibility that our society members should not shirk. Finally, I have one more hope, which is that everyone should raise more 'sons.' What I mean by 'sons' is not like what Mussolini and others advocate, which is to promote childbirth and increase the population. What I hope is that everyone can spiritually have more 'sons.' I am not just trying to drum up business for the Commercial Press and our colleagues; the publishing industry truly relies on everyone's leadership. The advancement of a country's culture is closely related to its independent survival. China's cultural undertakings and economic ideas definitely need to be promoted, so I sincerely hope that everyone can spiritually have more 'sons' and let the publishing industry shine." Liang Qingchun, director of the Hangzhou branch, then delivered a reply on behalf of the members, stating that, "Shanghai is not only an economic center but also a center of academic thought. Tonight's hosts are all leading figures in academia. Our society members should follow their example and shoulder the mission of developing Chinese academic culture to benefit the nation." The banquet concluded at around 9:00 PM with the guests and hosts parting on friendly terms.

Today's Excursion

According to the society's annual meeting schedule, members will be divided into groups today to visit scenic spots in Suzhou and Changshu. However, as it coincides with the traditional Mid-Autumn Festival, many members are staying in Shanghai for the holiday, so the number of participants in the excursion is not very large. Those participating in the Suzhou group include Chen Changheng and his wife, Yuan Zhao, Tang Qingzeng, Cao Lishun, Li Boqiang, Cui Xiaocen and his wife, Hu Qingrong, Li Quanshi, Lin Xijie, Zheng Zhao, Chen Heng, Xiong Lingxiao, and Li Yunliang, among others. The Changshu group includes Long Qida, Li Binghuan, Wang Zongpei, Wang Guang, Sheng Jun, Ding Jing, Li Bojia, Ding Shengbo, Fang Hao, and others. There may be additional last-minute joiners. According to inquiries at the society's office, all members participating in the excursion must gather at the society's office in the YMCA before 7:00 AM today to depart together.

Mayor's Banquet

Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng hosted a banquet for all members of the society at the City Hall auditorium in the city center yesterday at noon. Over 120 people attended, including Li Zhaohuan, Mu Ouchu, Wang Zhixin, Li Quanshi, Ma Yinchu, and Li Yunliang, among others. Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Secretaries Zhang Tingrong, Sun Pu, Zhang Yuanruo, and Section Chief Li Dachao accompanied the Mayor. During the banquet, the Mayor delivered a welcome speech, saying, "It is a great honor for the 13th annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society to be held in Shanghai. I deeply regret not being able to attend the opening ceremony due to other commitments. The society members are all economic experts and scholars who have come from afar from all parts of China, and I am very pleased. Shanghai is the economic center of China, and the relationship between various regions and Shanghai is close. I hope that you will guide the people of the whole country to carry out economic construction, promote the prosperity of Shanghai's people, and promote the prosperity of Shanghai and the revitalization of the rural areas in the interior. Society members gathered together to discuss economic issues, and I firmly believe that the future economic development of China is promising. Today, on behalf of the citizens of the city, I welcome everyone and fulfill the duties of a host. I am willing to receive everyone's guidance." Mu Ouchu then delivered a thank-you speech on behalf of the members, saying, "Today, we are honored to have Mayor Wu host a banquet, and I would like to thank you on behalf of all the members. The rapid progress of Shanghai's various constructions and the realization of the Greater Shanghai Plan are due to the Mayor's efforts. The magnificent constructions in the city center have been witnessed by all the members, so I hope that all the members will publicize the impressions of Shanghai's construction to the interior, and use Shanghai as a model to engage in construction. Although the Mayor has tried his best to find ways to alleviate the economic downturn in Shanghai's industry and commerce, it has not achieved its goal due to the harsh environment. It is expected that in another three to five years, the Mayor's Greater Shanghai Plan can be completed, and the Mayor's wishes can be fulfilled." A group photo was then taken before everyone dispersed.

Today is Mid-Autumn Festival - All Silver and Money Businesses are Closed - Foreign Exchange Rates Dropped Yesterday, Acceptance Notes Increased Sharply - All Industries Made Sufficient Preparations in Advance to Weather the Holiday

Shanghai's Industry and Commerce - The Mid-Autumn Festival settlement has arrived. The silver and money businesses were busy with collections and settlements yesterday, and all extended their hours. Today, they are all closed. The details are as follows:

Extended Hours - All factories, businesses, companies, and shops that handle collections and settlements are particularly busy these days as the Mid-Autumn Festival settlement has arrived. They have sent runners day and night to collect payments from customers. The Municipal Police Bureau and the police departments of the International Settlement and the French Concession have increased the number of detectives to protect the merchants collecting payments. The silver and money businesses were busy with collections and settlements yesterday, and all extended their office hours. Today, the guilds of both industries have notified all branches and affiliated organizations that they will be closed for one day.

Industries are Prepared to Weather the Holiday Safely - This year's Mid-Autumn Festival is different from previous years. Because all industries have learned from the economic downturn of previous years, they have made sufficient preparations in advance to avoid unfortunate events. The foreign exchange rate in the money market was 7 fen yesterday morning and afternoon, a decrease of 1 fen from the previous day, which is sufficient proof that the money supply in Shanghai is not tight. However, the total amount exchanged at the bank clearing house increased sharply yesterday, and the number of banks applying for acceptance notes at the bank acceptance house was higher than before.

Situation in Hongkou and Zhabei Increasingly Relaxed Yesterday - Municipal Council Offers 5,000 Yuan Reward for Arresting the Culprit

Central News Agency reports: The situation in the North Sichuan Road and the Zhabei Six-Three Garden and Baziqiao area yesterday was the same as the previous day. Japanese soldiers inside the Japanese brewery behind the Six-Three Garden have not yet withdrawn. According to nearby residents, dozens of Japanese soldiers inside the factory must travel back and forth to the Japanese barracks three times a day for meals (because there is no dining hall or other facilities inside the factory). Japanese military vehicles carrying Japanese soldiers can often be seen traveling back and forth for this reason. The open space next to the factory was originally a desolate vegetable garden, but after the Japanese soldiers were stationed there, it was leveled yesterday morning to create a flat training ground. The factory land is owned by Japanese businessmen, and the Japanese military authorities are currently negotiating with the businessmen to move out the family members living in the factory to facilitate a long-term stay. As for the Japanese cemetery in Baziqiao, because 80 to 90 Japanese residents went to pay their respects at 10:00 AM yesterday morning, the Japanese military authorities in Shanghai also sent ten soldiers to protect the area around the cemetery.

Xin Sheng News Agency reports: The situation in the Hongkou and Zhabei area gradually became peaceful yesterday. However, at around 7:00 AM, four Japanese military tanks, numbered 2, 3, 4, and 5, passed through Dixiwei Road, Qimei Road, Jiangwan Road, and Tongji Road. The Japanese troops at the wasteland at the end of Huayuan Street and the Tanaya Sake Brewery have not moved, and the coming and going of trucks has become commonplace. The construction work there has indeed been partially completed. For example, a watchtower has been built inside the Tanaya Sake Brewery, about four feet higher than the roof ridge, with a red lead sheet on top and a flagpole. The road at the end of Huayuan Street has also been extended to the wasteland and connected to the Tanaya Sake Brewery. According to eyewitnesses nearby, the Japanese troops have also dug two wells inside the factory, because there is no tap water there. At around 9:00 AM, 60 to 70 Japanese students, divided into three large trucks, were escorted by Japanese military motorcycles to visit. Later, the group of students also went to the Japanese cemetery in Baziqiao. Japanese soldiers patrolled Jiangwan Road, and three Japanese soldiers were stationed at the intersection of Tongji Road and Jiangwan Road, but they withdrew after 5:00 PM. As for the Japanese military outposts at the Yongfeng Building on North Sichuan Road, the intersection of Dixiwei Road and Damei Road, and the Japanese Girls' School on Ouchang Road, as well as the patrolling of other roads, the situation was the same as the previous days, with no special circumstances. The various situations are reported as follows:

One Japanese Warship Leaves Shanghai Yesterday

Dagong News Agency reports: The No. 3 Japanese warship, which sailed to Hankou the day before yesterday, sailed to the Japanese naval pontoon bridge at Lan Ni Du in Pudong to berth, load coal, and refuel. One of them has now sailed out of the Wusongkou at 4:10 PM yesterday and headed upstream of the Yangtze River. The four torpedo boats No. 22 and the two Japanese warships No. 3 on the Jiangmian of the NingShao Wharf at Xiaodongmen, which are moored at the Mitsui Wharf in Pudong, are also firing up and waiting to depart. However, as of last night, they had not yet set sail. The Kumano, Fuyo, Asagao, and other three warships from South China did not arrive in Shanghai yesterday.

Municipal Council Offers a Heavy Reward to Arrest the Culprit

Zi Lin Daily reports: The Municipal Council's Police Department offered a reward of 5,000 yuan on Sunday to arrest the perpetrator who shot and killed one Japanese sailor and seriously injured two sailors on Wednesday night in Hongkou. Anyone who provides information leading to the arrest of the real perpetrator will be rewarded with this amount. According to Vice Superintendent and Special Political Officer of the Municipal Council Police Department, Japanese national Ta Jima (transliteration), when interviewed by a reporter yesterday (28th), claimed that the personnel investigating the murder case are working hard. However, they cannot disclose the nature of everything they have found out. He is very hopeful about the results of the investigation. The panic in Hongkou in the past few days has gradually disappeared, so the area appears to be quiet on the surface. The Japanese schools in the area and in Zhabei have resumed classes yesterday after being suspended for three days.

Japanese Residents Request More Plainclothes Police

Nichinichi Mainichi Shimbun reports: At 4:00 PM on the 28th, the Shanghai Japanese Road Association held a committee meeting at the Japanese Club. In view of the urgency of the current situation, they discussed countermeasures. As a result of the agreement, they decided to petition the Municipal Council to increase the number of Japanese plainclothes police and to replace the heads of the Hongkou and Dixiwei Road police stations with Japanese nationals.

Worker Detained for Throwing Longan Shells

Da Mei Evening News reports: On Sunday night, a worker named Li from the Xingli Bakery at No. 172 Yuqing Lane, North Sichuan Road, threw longan shells out of the window, unintentionally hitting a passing Japanese sailor. The sailor immediately reported it to the Public Security Bureau, and the police rushed to detain the owner of the bakery and the worker. Fortunately, two Japanese neighbors testified that the worker had thrown the shells unintentionally. However, for the sake of caution, the Public Security Bureau must wait until the Japanese naval officer expresses satisfaction with the testimony of the two Japanese neighbors before releasing the detained worker. It is expected that he will be released this afternoon (29th).

Two Mas Detained Request Assistance

Xin Sheng News Agency reports: Two workers from the Hongxing Zhangji Printing House, Ma Yongshou and Ma Yongnian, were detained by Japanese soldiers at the Japanese military headquarters on the 23rd of this month on their way home from work, on suspicion of assassinating Japanese soldiers. They are now being transferred to the court and have lost their freedom. The manager of the printing house, Lan Sheng, sent a special letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Public Concession requesting assistance. The letter reads: "We respectfully inform you that two brothers, Ma Yongshou and Ma Yongnian, printing workers at our printing house, were detained by Japanese soldiers at the Japanese military headquarters at the intersection of Haining Road and Wusong Road at 8:00 PM on the 23rd of this month on their way home from work. They were falsely accused of being suspects in the assassination of Japanese soldiers. On the 24th, they were handed over to the Hongkou Police Station. In the afternoon of the 24th, the police personnel escorted the two Ma brothers to our printing house for questioning. Our printing house confirmed that they were indeed workers at our printing house and had been safely working at our company before being arrested on 23rd. After our printing house's manager, Wang Lansheng, personally went to the Hongkou Police Station to apply for bail, it was rejected. On the morning of the 25th at 9:00 AM, the Hongkou Police Station transferred the case to the First Special District Court for trial. The court ruled that they should be detained for one week for investigation and further interrogation. We believe that the two Ma brothers have always been peaceful workers, with an elderly mother in her sixties and wives, children, and grandchildren below. A family of more than ten people relies entirely on the work of the two brothers to make a living. Once they are arrested and detained innocently, the livelihood of the entire family will inevitably be cut off. Therefore, we specially write to your esteemed association, hoping that you will consider that they have been unfairly burdened and that your esteemed association will protect the rights and interests of the citizens of the concession and the minimum principles of safety for residence and travel. We ask that you quickly send a letter to the Police Department of the Municipal Council and the First Special District Court, requesting a speedy investigation and bail to avoid them being unjustly burdened. This is a matter of public concern."

Mr. and Mrs. Jiang Huaben (Photo by International News Agency)

Jiang Huaben Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday and Will Report to Beijing Soon

Jiang Huaben, the Consul General stationed in Kobe, Japan, was transferred back to China to serve as a member of the Treaty Committee of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. He arrived in Shanghai at 11:30 AM yesterday, accompanied by his wife, on the Japanese postal ship Tatsuta Maru. The chief of the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Zhou Jue, and many relatives and friends of Jiang went to the wharf to welcome them. After landing, they went to their accommodations to rest. It is also learned that Kan'nou, the head of the Japanese Residents' Association in Shanghai, returned to Japan at the beginning of the month to report on the situation, which has now been completed, and also returned to Shanghai on the same ship yesterday. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency met Jiang on the ship yesterday and discussed the following:

Overseas Chinese Commerce

The scope of the Kobe Consulate General is relatively wide, covering Osaka, Kyoto, Nagoya, and other places, all under the jurisdiction of the Kobe Consulate General. At present, there are more than 10,000 overseas Chinese in the entire area. Regarding overseas Chinese commerce, most are import and export merchants. Osaka mainly deals with the three northeastern provinces, Ping, Tianjin, and Qingdao in China, while Kobe mainly deals with various British and Dutch territories in Nanyang. In terms of scale, most are joint ventures, lacking company organizations, and their operations are mainly to transport Japanese goods for export. The import goods to China are almost all raw materials, such as medicinal materials, cotton, and cowhide. Since the emergence of the so-called "Manchukuo," the dealings between Osaka and China have mostly been replaced by Japanese people, which has had a considerable impact. At the same time, various territories in Nanyang have recently restricted Japanese goods, and the Japanese have taken the initiative to find ways to promote sales. The dealings between overseas Chinese in Kobe and Nanyang have also been greatly affected.

Chinese Workers Being Expelled

As for the overseas Chinese who have been expelled back to China in the past, most belong to the working class, such as dock workers, cloth peddlers, barbers, and cooks. According to Japanese law, all laborers must obtain permission, otherwise they will be ordered to leave the country. Most of these overseas Chinese lack knowledge and are not proficient in the Japanese language, so they are often forced to return to China. Regarding overseas Chinese education, there are currently three overseas Chinese schools in Kobe, and one each in Osaka and Kyoto.

China-Japan Relations

I believe that whether the relationship between the two countries is friendly depends on the feelings between the people of the two countries. If the people's feelings are good, then the national relationship can be harmonious. Otherwise, the national relationship will inevitably deteriorate. The current relationship between China and Japan is no exception. Japan is now promoting amity. I have sincerely told Japanese reporters that empty talk is useless. If the two countries want amity, they must be open and honest, and be able to sincerely put it into practice. I left after Mr. Wang Shoushan, the new appointee, arrived and completed the handover. Before leaving, I was unable to visit Ambassador Xu in Tokyo. After staying in Shanghai for a short period of time, I will go to Beijing to report to Foreign Minister Zhang and return to the ministry to take up my post.

City Chamber of Commerce Continues to Submit Donations for Purchasing Airplanes from Various Guilds - Tenth Batch - Aviation Fees for Civil Aviation Industry - Changed Collection Method

Various groups and individuals in the city enthusiastically support the movement to purchase airplanes to celebrate the birthday, and they are actively donating. Details have been reported in various newspapers. The Shanghai Purchase Airplane Commemorative Committee has continued to receive the tenth batch of donations from the City Chamber of Commerce, totaling 1,600 yuan, including 1,000 yuan from the Fruit and Local Produce Industry Guild, 200 yuan from the Cotton Merchant Guild, 50 yuan from the Tea Industry Guild, 45 yuan from the Clear Oil and Rapeseed Industry Guild, and 605 yuan raised by the Woolen Fabric Factory Industry Guild, including 50 yuan each from Dadong Factory, Dade Factory, Huadong Factory, and Patriotic Factory, 20 yuan from Tongyi Factory, 15 yuan from Huadong employees, and 10 yuan each from Tianhe Factory, Tiansheng Factory, Jinglun Factory, Shenchang Factory, and Dada Factory, and 5 yuan each from Shengda Factory, Gongchang Factory, Jianchang Factory, and Daxing Factory. All have been acknowledged and thanked.

The entire city's shipping industry previously proposed collecting aviation fees to support the aviation salvation movement. The head of the China Aviation Association's General Team Office convened a meeting with the industry to discuss the matter and obtained the approval of the Shanghai Municipal Government for issuance. It started on December 10th of last year, but the results were mediocre. Starting in May of this year, it was requested that the Treasury Department's Ship Tax Office collect the fees on its behalf. The details have been reported in various newspapers. In order to reduce the burden on the shipping industry, the General Team Leader Office specially wrote to the Treasury Department, inviting the Fengguan Section and the heads of various ship tax offices to discuss the matter at the department at 2:00 PM on the 15th. The meeting was chaired by General Secretary Li Dachao, who decided on the spot to collect the aviation fees only once and have the Ship Tax Office continue to collect them on its behalf. The Municipal Government was requested to issue a notice, and the Public Security Bureau's water patrol team was requested to assist. The collection standards were set at 5 jiao for first to second class ships, 1 yuan for third to fifth class ships, 2 yuan for sixth to eighth class ships, and 3 yuan for ninth to twelfth class ships. The collection period is from October 1st to the end of November. All civilian ships in Shanghai must be collected on schedule. It is heard that the Municipal Government has approved the record and issued a notice, which will officially start tomorrow.

Baihe River Water Level Drops, Fenpu Runs Aground, Only 13 Feet at the Lightship, Ships Dispatched to Unload Cargo

The Fenpu, a vessel of the Sanbei Shipping Company, with a load capacity of 1,910 tons and a draft of 17 feet 2 inches, was transporting miscellaneous grains, flour, etc. from Shanghai to Tianjin. On the 28th, it sailed into Dagukou. At 10:00 AM, when it sailed into the Baihe River near the lightship, the water level was only 13 feet, and the Fenpu ran aground. It telegraphed the Tianjin branch to dispatch barges to unload the cargo from the ship in order to refloat itself. It is now said that the water level in the Baihe River is only 12 feet.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Restores Inland River Machine Factory, Commissioner Lan Jian Departs for Hankou Today

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's inland river machine factory, since the Shanghai factory ceased operations in April of this year, has moved all machinery and other items to Hankou in order to repair the Yangtze River vessels. The factory site in Shanghai is certainly not as convenient as in Hankou. Now, the factory's machines are still intact and well-maintained, and efforts are being made to resume operations in order to provide repairs for the bureau's vessels. The complete statistics for the restoration of various machines, the layout of the Hankou factory site, and the configuration of spare parts and required projects have been carefully reviewed and calculated by the bureau, requiring more than 93,000 yuan. With the approval of the ministry, the bureau has specially appointed Zhou Houkun, deputy director of the bureau's shipping department, and Zhuo Jun, commissioner of the inland river machine factory, as supervisors of the factory's restoration. All procedures have been negotiated with Cao Shoulian, director of the inland river machine factory, in recent days. Mr. Zhou and Mr. Zhuo are scheduled to take the bureau's river vessel to Hankou today to implement the supervision of the inland river machine factory's restoration work. All factory workers, in addition to a portion who will travel from Shanghai, will be hired in Hankou.

Two Detainees Escape, Guard Sentenced, 50 Days Detention

Jiang Wanyuan, a bailiff from the Fifth Division of the Second Special District Court, originally from Yangzhou, was escorting criminal detainees to the waiting room behind the First Tribunal on the morning of the 15th of this month, awaiting trial, when he carelessly left the key to the door in the lock of the back door of the waiting room. As a result, the detainees Wu Asan and Wang Agen seized the opportunity to use the key to open the back door, pry open the iron gate on the iron fence, and escape without a trace at around 2:00 PM. When it was discovered, there was no way to pursue them. The foreign chief judicial constable reported to the president of the court, and Bailiff Jiang was detained and transferred to the Prosecutor's Office. Prosecutor Wang Ren concluded the investigation and filed a public prosecution against Jiang in the criminal court for the crime of negligent escape under Article 163, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. Judge Chen Shuoying, together with the prosecutor, held a court hearing and concluded the inquiry. The circumstances of the scheduled pronouncement of the sentence have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday, the judgment was delivered. At 2:00 PM, Judge Chen and Prosecutor Wang arrived at Criminal Tribunal 2, ordered the defendant Jiang Wanyuan to be brought to the case, briefly questioned his age and origin, and then announced the judgment: Jiang Wanyuan was sentenced to 50 days of detention. Jiang immediately declared that he accepted the judgment and waived the right to appeal. The official then ordered him to be returned to custody to await execution.

Li Zicheng, originally from Ningbo, formerly partnered with Yu Zuoting, Qi Ziquan, Sun Jieqing, Ye Zengshou, and Xue Chunsheng to open the Jin Tai Money Exchange at No. 8 Zhongde Lane, 449 Beijing Road. Recently, the Xinyuan Money Exchange, through a lawyer, filed a lawsuit in the First Special District Court against Jin Tai Exchange and Li Zicheng, among others, seeking compensation for damages. The grounds for the lawsuit were that Xinyuan had invested 30,000 yuan in Jin Tai Exchange and several Ningbo money exchanges to jointly establish Yongtai Company, specializing in the pawn business.

In November of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, the title deed for Sun Chunsheng's two mu, one li, and one hao of land was received as a pawn. Last year, Jin Tai secretly pledged it to the Central Bank, obtaining 340,000 yuan. Therefore, the lawsuit was filed. During the ongoing litigation, Li Zicheng examined the red account books of Jin Tai Exchange for previous years and found no accounts for joint investment in Shui Tai Company, nor any record of pledging the Yongtai pawned title deed to the Central Bank.

Repercussions of the Municipal Council's Increased Donation Rates, Yongchangtai Customs Brokerage Firm Asks the Ratepayers Association for Support

The Guomin News Agency reports that the Yongtai Chang Customs Brokerage Firm, located at 22 Changgeng Lane, 158 Edward Road, in the Public Concession, sent a letter to the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Public Concession, stating: "Respectfully, our firm has leased a municipal house at No. 22, Lane 158, Edward Road, since February 1st of this year, with a monthly rent of 500 yuan. According to the current regulations of the Municipal Council, the annual municipal general donation should be 840 yuan. However, the Municipal Council is either unaware of the high rents of the past, or mistakenly believes that the cost of business equipment and decoration is a prepaid rent for an additional burden, or misunderstands Article 5 of the contract, and arbitrarily assesses the value of our firm's rent and forcibly increases it. In order to protect the interests of taxpayers and respect the current donation rate, our firm has repeatedly argued on reasonable grounds, but has ultimately failed to obtain the understanding of the Municipal Council. We hereby present the circumstances to your association." We believe that the leaders of our Chinese taxpayers association will be able to uphold justice and safeguard the rights and interests of our Chinese taxpayers. Initially, the Municipal Council notified our firm to come for a discussion, stating that our firm's house donation must be paid according to the donation amount before February 1st. Later, it said that at least it must be paid according to an annual rent of 8,000 yuan. Then, it said that out of consideration for the difficulties of business, it would be reduced to an annual rent of 7,400 yuan. After hearing this, our firm was extremely shocked. The Municipal Council should collect taxes according to the regulations. How can it arbitrarily change them? We immediately explained the actual situation to the bureau and explained the misunderstanding. However, the Municipal Council sent a letter on April 20th, stating that the donation amount must be calculated according to a monthly rent of 625 yuan. The reasons given were: "(1) When the Municipal Council believes that the rent does not match the value of the house, it has the right to re-estimate its value and collect taxes; (2) Although the lease states that the monthly rent is 500 yuan, there is an additional burden of 3,000 yuan for business equipment and decoration, which must be included in the total rent." After further explanation by letter, and submitting a copy of the lease contract and various documents regarding the 3,000 yuan for business equipment and decoration for reference, the bureau misunderstood the meaning of Article 5 of the contract, insisting that this 3,000 yuan was a prepaid rent. Although repeated letters were sent, it was not understood. In fact, this 3,000 yuan is the price our firm paid to the former tenant, Tiantaicheng Customs Brokerage Firm, for business equipment and decoration, which initially had nothing to do with the landlord, and there is no obligation to return it to the landlord when the lease expires. Article 5 of the lease states that decorations that come with the house may not be removed after expiration, otherwise, they must be restored to their original form. The reason why they are not allowed to be removed is actually a modified condition for the original tenant to restore the decorations to their original form before taking over. Moreover, business equipment and decoration are different, and a large part of this 3,000 yuan is the price of business equipment and decoration, so it should be distinguished and cannot be confused. The Municipal Council misunderstands again and again, ignores the decline of the market, the sharp drop in rents, and insists on going its own way, which is not a way to be considerate of the difficulties of business. Now the amount of our firm's rent has been confirmed by the court based on the rent value of neighboring houses, and the Municipal Council's valuation is considered to be legitimate. We have already appealed this seemingly correct argument. Please consider the situation and uphold justice, then the beneficiaries will not only be our firm, but also the residents and shops in this concession will all benefit. Otherwise, the Municipal Council will arbitrarily increase or decrease the tax based on one-sided views, and the harm will be endless. We are sending copies of our firm's correspondence with the Municipal Council and our appeal letter, and respectfully request your association to provide assistance. We deeply hope and pray for this. To the Shanghai Public Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association."

Municipal Council Designated Hospitals Offer Free Smallpox Vaccinations

Now that summer has passed and autumn has arrived, the weather is unpredictable, and smallpox often occurs in children. If mild, it can cause pockmarks and blindness, and if severe, it can lead to death. Matters of life and death should not be ignored. Therefore, the authorities are devising ways to provide relief. The Public Concession Municipal Council Health Department has now designated the Hongkou Civilian Obstetrics Hospital and the Chinese Hospital to provide completely free smallpox vaccinations starting on October 1st. These two hospitals have always been charitable, and even pregnant women with limited funds who come to the hospital to give birth can receive free care and daily medical treatment. This time, the smallpox vaccine is fresh. Parents of all circles should fulfill their responsibility to protect their children and not be negligent. The hospital's telephone number is 50936, and it is located at the intersection of Ward Road in Tilanqiao.

Renji Hospital, August Report

Renji Hospital's August report for this year states: Outpatient numbers: 16,623; New inpatients: 365; Total inpatient days: 6,411; Average daily meals served: 460; Male suicide attempts: 56; Female suicide attempts: 53; Emergency surgeries: 433; Emergency surgeries due to factory accidents: 31; Patients sent by the Public Concession police: 513; Patients sent by the French Concession police: 79; Deliveries: 23. Judging from the above statistics, the hospital's work in August was roughly equivalent to that of the previous month. Among the above categories, some slightly increased compared to July, while others slightly decreased. The utilization of the obstetrics department has shown significant popularization effects. Delivery numbers were ten in July and have increased to 23 in August. In addition to the increased record of delivery numbers, the hospital serves the entire community by providing a prenatal clinic for pregnant women. Some pregnant women come to the hospital for consultation several months before delivery, while others book beds two months in advance. During the antepartum period, pregnant women receive thorough diagnosis, treatment, and guidance from the hospital. A pediatric health check clinic has also been established within the obstetrics department. Parents are often seen bringing their babies to the clinic for check-ups. The hospital staff observes the progress of the babies' health and provides guidance on common infant care methods, such as bathing and feeding, making a significant contribution to the well-being of society, especially infants. The nursing training school admitted 17 new female students in August. The class must undergo a short probationary period before being formally admitted to receive full nursing training. Miss Goole has worked diligently for five years and has now been granted leave and left Shanghai. However, Miss Evans has joined the senior nursing staff. Miss Evans recently completed a one-year course at the Suzhou Language School. The hospital's board of directors has been studying the hospital's financial situation and is quite concerned because the hospital relies heavily on property income. Recently, due to the economic downturn in the city, tenants have often failed to pay rent on time. The hospital’s economic income for this year, up to the present time, has decreased by 21% compared to the same period last year, which is a serious situation. They are now trying their best to balance income and expenditure.

Since the Dongjiadu ferry across the river began operating on March 1st of this year, it has been fast and safe, which is convenient for passengers. The wharf and ferry equipment there were originally capable of transporting cars, but because the section of road from Tangqiao Road to Pudong Avenue had not yet been completed, cars could not travel back and forth. It is learned that the section of road and bridge has been widened and completed by the Public Works Bureau. Recently, passenger cars from Puxi to Pudong can be transported across the river by ferry at Dongjiadu and drive directly to various districts in Pudong. The route will operate from 2:00 AM to 11:00 PM from October 1st, with ten round trips per hour. Each car crossing the river will be charged 100 copper coins. Regardless of the rise and fall of the tide during sailing hours, it can be loaded. From now on, residents of Pudong and those visiting Pudong can travel directly by car from Puxi, which is very convenient.

Trademark Bureau Handles Guangdong Trademark Measures

The Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry issued a circular stating that it had received Instruction No. 47919 of the Ministry of Industry stating, "In order to unify the handling of company, trademark, franchise, fishery, mining, accountant, technician, and assistant technician, fishing boat captain, and fishing captain cases in Guangdong, the Ministry has specially stipulated the Interim Measures for Handling Cases in Guangdong Handled by the Ministry of Industry, which were announced on September 5 this year. One item of the measures, regarding trademark cases, is from Article 4 to Article 9, a total of six articles, and two supplementary provisions, which are copied and sent to the bureau for compliance." The relevant articles of the Interim Measures for Handling Cases in Guangdong Handled by the Ministry of Industry regarding trademark cases are copied below, from Article 4 to Article 9, and Supplementary Provisions 18 and 19, for everyone to know. Furthermore, the former Guangdong Commissioner's Office of this Bureau has been ordered to be abolished and closed at the end of February this year. There are no document collection agencies in Guangdong Province. All trademark cases should be submitted directly to the Bureau at Moling Road in the capital. This is hereby announced. Copy of the Interim Measures for Handling Cases in Guangdong Handled by the Ministry of Industry, announced on September 5, 1936, one item regarding trademark cases: (4) Those who have obtained a trademark registration certificate from the Guangdong local government after May 1929 shall submit the original certificate along with ten copies of the trademark design, one printing plate, and one yuan of stamp duty to the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry for review in accordance with the law. The registration fee is waived. (5) Trademarks submitted for review in accordance with the preceding paragraph may be ordered to be modified within a time limit if they must be rejected. Only one modification is allowed. If the trademark is still illegal after modification, it will be rejected and the stamp duty paid will be returned. (6) If a trademark is rejected by the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and another trademark is submitted for registration, the registration fees shall be paid separately in accordance with the law. (7) Trademarks that have not been registered, regardless of whether they are submitted or published, shall not be effective. They shall be submitted to the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry for registration separately in accordance with the law. (8) Trademark oppositions or judgments handled by the Guangdong local government shall not be effective. (9) Those who do not obtain a registration certificate from the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry in accordance with these measures shall not have the exclusive right to use the trademark under the originally obtained trademark registration certificate from the Guangdong local government. Supplementary Provisions: 18. The exchange of licenses, certificates, or registration certificates stipulated in these measures shall be limited to December 31, 1936. After the deadline, all cases shall be handled as new cases. 19. These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

After the collapse of Tongyi Trust Company, in addition to those that have already been judged, there are still three cases in which all directors and supervisors were accused of violating the Company Law and the Savings Bank Law, etc., filed by Lu Tangcha and others. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Ye Bichao of the First Special District District Court continued to hear the case. Only four defendants, Xu Jiqun, Zhou Shouliang, Guo Yushang, and Chuan Zhuyin, surrendered themselves. Jiang Liuzhi still claimed to be ill and was represented in court by a lawyer. The remaining defendants, Huang Suchu, etc., were nowhere to be found. The court questioned Xu and others once, and then ordered the debate to begin. First, the lawyers Zhang Yifan and others for the plaintiffs spoke, stating that there is no distinction in the Company Law between performing business and not performing business. All directors must bear equal responsibility. Then, Xu Shihaho, the defense lawyer for the two defendants Xu and Zhou, defended Xu and Zhou, saying that Xu and Zhou were ordinary directors and were not responsible for all actions within the company. He requested that they be declared not guilty. If the court believes that they are not without criminal suspicion, they are also continuous offenders, and the various charges sued in this case have all been judged in the previous case. In terms of procedure, this case can be prosecuted and should not be accepted. Then, the lawyer for Guo Yushang defended Guo, which was roughly similar to what Xu's lawyer said. Finally, the lawyers for the two defendants Jiang and Chuan defended, saying that Jiang and Chuan were supervisors, and the accusations made by the plaintiffs were mostly against directors, and their duties were irrelevant to the supervisors, etc. After the debate, Judge Ye ordered that the judgment be announced next Friday.

New Invention, Electric Essence Lamp Born

Gao Jinshan and Weng Renyong from Zhejiang, feeling that villages and towns without power plants are not as brightly lit as large cities late at night, which hinders municipal development, transportation, popularization of education, etc., were determined to find a way to solve this problem. After immersing themselves in research, they invented an electric essence lamp last spring. The style is no different from the current electric lamp, but it does not require dry batteries or hydroelectric power, nor does it need gasoline or kerosene. The installation does not need to be fixed at a location and can be moved at will. The strength and switching on and off of the light can all be done as desired. It is exquisite, ingenious, simple, and economical, and is still a novel invention in the world. From now on, remote rural areas can be brightly lit, and travel will not be afraid of darkness. It can truly be called a new invention that benefits the country and the people. Since Gao and Weng organized the Guangming Electric Essence Lamp Factory and set up a distribution office in the Renli district of Nanyang Ju Nandun in this city, it is heard that distributors from all over the country have come in droves, and supply cannot meet demand. The factory has great difficulty coping with the situation. This is also good news for domestic goods.

Her relationship with her husband is usually quite harmonious, but she has disagreements with her father-in-law, Zong Shaofu, and aunt, Zong Wang. Therefore, quarrels often occur. Yesterday morning, they quarreled again over trivial matters, angering Zong Wang, which caused her to become angry and beat her daughter-in-law with a wooden stick, causing her to be covered in injuries. Zong Chen reported to the police officer accusing her father-in-law and aunt of abuse. The three defendants, along with the wooden stick, were taken to the station for questioning. Foreign Shareholders of Meihua Bank Rejected in Lawsuit Because Foreign Shareholders Are Not Victims, They Are Not Allowed to File a Private Prosecution According to Law

After the collapse of Meihua Bank, which was founded by Gu Yubo and others, the foreign shareholder and chairman of the bank, Englishman Meng Lei, and the shareholders and directors Yale and Malaito, etc., originally each subscribed for one share, but they did not pay a penny of their 100 yuan share capital. In fact, the three of them did not suffer any losses. However, they jointly filed a criminal private prosecution against Gu Yubo, Chen Yizai, and Bao Ziwen, Chinese shareholders, in the First Special District District Court for breach of trust and fraud, and also filed a related civil suit, demanding compensation for losses. After repeated court hearings, because Gu had absconded, he had been wanted. Although Chen and Bao had not surrendered, the matters sued by Meng Lei and others had been thoroughly investigated and the case was concluded. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng held a court session and announced the main text of the judgment, stating that the case would not be accepted and the lawsuit of the plaintiff in the related civil suit was rejected. Judge Huang also briefly stated the reasons in court, saying that because the private prosecutor was not the victim, he was not allowed to file a private prosecution according to law, so it should not be accepted.

Tenth Inspection Report of the Issuance Reserve Management Committee

The Issuance Reserve Management Committee issued its tenth inspection announcement stating that, in accordance with the provisions of Article 7 of the committee's charter, on September 26, 1936, the committee inspected the issuance reserves of the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) Total issuance of the Central Bank of China: 31,343,551.63 yuan; Total reserve: 31,343,551.63 yuan, including 11,127,406.3 yuan in cash reserve and 10,216,110 yuan in security reserve. (B) Total issuance of the Bank of China: 37,776,842.592 yuan; Total reserve: 37,776,842.592 yuan, including 23,837,513.285 yuan in cash reserve and 13,939,329.307 yuan in security reserve. (C) Total issuance of the Bank of Communications: 21,711,041 yuan; Total reserve: 21,711,041 yuan, including 15,194,318.1 yuan in cash reserve and 6,516,723 yuan in security reserve. Total issuance: 90,831,399.92 yuan; Total reserve: 90,831,399.92 yuan, including 60,159,176.85 yuan in cash reserve and 30,672,623.07 yuan in security reserve. The above issuance and reserve amounts, cash reserve exceeding 60% and security reserve below 40%, are in compliance with the committee's inspection rules. This is hereby announced. Issuance Reserve Management Committee.

Central Bank Inspection Report

The 302nd Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserve of the Central Bank's Convertible Notes states: This committee, in accordance with Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, is responsible for inspecting the number of convertible notes issued by the bank and its reserve funds. The 302nd inspection was held at the bank's Issuance Bureau on September 26, 1936. The results of the inspection are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued is 31,343,916.63 silver dollars, including 27,912,283 silver dollar notes and 1,431,233.33 subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of convertible note reserves is 31,343,516.63 silver dollars, including 21,127,406.63 silver dollars in cash reserves. The cash reserve includes 9,786,913.22 silver dollars stored in the bank's issuing branches and sub-branches, and 11,340,040.71 silver dollars stored in other banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 10,216,110 silver dollars. (B) The amount of Customs Gold Unit convertible notes issued is 400,963.07 Customs Gold Units. The total amount of Customs Gold Unit convertible note reserves is 400,963.07 Customs Gold Units. The reserve includes 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, valued at 51.68, totaling 400,963.07 Customs Gold Units. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the current reserve should be at least 60%, with the remainder guaranteed by legal collateral. The inspection results show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guarantee reserve is within 40%, which complies with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. September 28, 1936, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fusun, Supervisor Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiji.

Zhao Yu-Huang's New Book on Pharmacy Published

Domestic medicinal materials have the most scientific research value and are the most complex and chaotic, making research the most difficult. In recent years, there have been many people in China studying Chinese medicine, but most do not pay attention to the study of pharmacognosy and instead engage in pharmaceutical chemistry and pharmacology. This has led to many errors in the basic problems of Chinese medicine without being noticed. This is a huge obstacle in medicine. Mr. Zhao Yu-Huang has been devoted to this field for thirty years. Since leaving Academia Sinica and being hired by the Peking Research Institute, he has begun to organize medicinal materials from North China, collecting more than 2,800 specimens. He uses the latest research methods of pharmacognosy to verify and discover with ancient herbal texts, laying a scientific foundation for China's thousands of years of traditional medicine and increasing its efficiency. This is a great contribution to the study of Chinese medicine. The results of the research have been published in the first volume of "Qizhou Medicinal Materials," a study of the pharmacognosy of the Compositae and Dipsacaceae (Umbelliferae) families. A total of twelve volumes have been successfully studied. The first volume is priced at four yuan and is published by the Publishing Department of the Peking Research Institute.

Shen Bao National Products Special Issue

Eliminating Unhealthy Psychological Attitudes of Housewives in the National Products Movement

— Cheng Xuan

(1) Greed for Cheapness: Taking advantage is a common unhealthy psychological attitude shared by both men and women. Money should be cherished, and goods should be chosen for their low price. However, the opposite of cheapness is loss, and cheapness and loss are proportional. In other words, cheapness is equal to loss. If cheapness and loss are not equal, then it is not cheapness. We know that the National Products Movement and housewives have a close relationship, and women's greed for cheapness is even more severe than men's. Therefore, when they see goods that are new in design, fashionable, and cheap in price, they ultimately do not distinguish whether they are domestic products or not and buy them casually. Unscrupulous merchants take advantage of their greed for cheapness to obtain money. As a result, money flows out of the country in countless amounts. In fact, this unhealthy psychological attitude is too harmful to the national livelihood and can be said to be worse than the trade deficit. You must know that if you are greedy for some cheapness, you will suffer a great loss in economic invasion, becoming an inverse proportion. This is a small matter, but you will also receive the gifts of enemy artillery fire and bombs! Isn't that greatly not cheap? Therefore, I sincerely advise those who have a greedy heart, for the sake of national livelihood and the future, and for the sake of the National Products Movement, if you do not want to be slaves, swear to eradicate and thoroughly change this unhealthy psychological attitude of greed for cheapness. Housewives! You should especially correct it if you have it, and encourage yourself if you don't!

(2) Complacency: You must not be complacent about anything, especially not about national products. If a person gets used to complacency, they will be careless. Moreover, now that smuggled goods are rampant and counterfeit goods are rampant, if you are also complacent! Who cares if it is a domestic product or not! Just buy it and be done with it. You must know that if you are so complacent, it will be terrible! To be honest, such a large China can also be lost on the word "complacency"! Complacency is to fail to fulfill the national duty and not to fulfill the national obligation. You must know that "everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world." Adopting domestic products and not buying non-domestic products is one of the national defense policies, so everyone must do it. Housewives buying non-domestic products due to complacency is unknown in China, where education and knowledge are not widespread. I hope that knowledgeable housewives will not only encourage themselves but also promote and advise other housewives. Moreover, although parents are both role models for children, mothers occupy an important position. Upon careful examination, most housewives and children linger at foreign toy stalls and shops, and complacently buy foreign goods to satisfy children's childish desires. Isn't this harming the future of children and also a result of the unhealthy psychological effect of "complacency"? This kind of influence expands its power invisibly and is really hard to guard against! The above two points are very simple to say and everyone knows and feels them, but it is often easy to violate them like being infected by what you see and hear. The foundation of domestic products must be laid well. I hope housewives will pay attention to it.

A Few Words of Contribution

A Dedicated Speech for the National Products Exhibition of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

— Yang An

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce is holding a large-scale National Products Exhibition at the International Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road to commemorate the 15th anniversary of the Commodity Exhibition Hall. More than 150 manufacturers are participating, and the opening is scheduled for October 1st. It is of great significance that a legitimate industrial and commercial group is holding this grand gathering during this critical period of national crisis. In addition to our joy, we would like to offer three points to the people of Shanghai and the gentlemen who are hosting this event.

(1) Observe this Exhibition with a Progressive Perspective: The products in this exhibition have improved rapidly compared to previous exhibitions. Some products, which were previously not produced domestically, are now on display at the exhibition, gradually reaching a state of self-sufficiency from the process of relying on imports. Although it is still not perfect due to material resources, talent, and financial resources, it is fair to say that the domestic products industry has been able to struggle and fight amidst countless hardships to achieve this kind of achievement. If given more time, on the one hand, they will gather talents to improve technology, and on the other hand, they will provide financial assistance to ensure sufficient strength. The achievements will be immeasurable. This is the first point.

(2) Promote the Improvement of National Products with Honest Criticism: It is heard that after the exhibition, experts will be invited to conduct a review as a preparation for awards. We believe that the criticism of a few people is not as good as the criticism of many people. Using the eyes of the public, which is superior, which is secondary, what should be improved, and what should be changed? We hope that the gentlemen attending the exhibition will provide honest criticism for the reference of each factory to improve. This is of great importance to promoting the progress of industry. We hope that the people of Shanghai will pay attention to it.

(3) Do Your Best to Promote National Products with a Loving Mentality: We are very gratified to see so many products and so much progress in the domestic products industry. If there are any shortcomings, we should forgive them and do our best to promote them and open up avenues for them with a mentality of loving domestic products. Identify the primary importance of saving the country in promoting domestic products, and treat the producers with respect and love, giving them sufficient progress and full development, and then complete the national duty. All three points should be understood by the domestic products industry itself, which should also understand the importance of its own responsibility, strive for excellence, and strive for beauty to compete with foreign goods, so that the holding of this exhibition will be more meaningful.

The Mid-Autumn Festival and National Products

— Qing Bo

The clock hand is like a bird in the sky, flying away in an instant, and finally disappearing without a trace.

Memories of the Mid-Autumn Festival of youth seem to be still in front of us, and this year's Mid-Autumn Festival has quickly arrived again in an instant. The rapid passage of time really gives us young people endless feelings.

These few days, if we have free time, we can stroll around the streets. Then, you will surely see many people crowding in and out of major companies, holding bundles and packages in their hands. What are these people busy with? What exactly are they busy with? The author is really inexplicable. Then I thought: That's right! That's right! The Mid-Autumn Festival is coming in a few days, and people are rational and emotional animals. How can they not buy some things to send to their dear relatives and friends to express the friendship between the two parties?

Indeed, "Every festive season brings more thoughts of loved ones!" For the sons who are wandering outside for a living, now that the Mid-Autumn Festival is about to arrive, they should indeed buy some things to take home to please their parents and comfort their wives and young children. This is also human nature, and can we give them any criticism?

However, fellow citizens who are purchasing gifts: We must know, what era is this? How serious is our economic national crisis now? How serious is the invasion of foreign goods and the rampant smuggling of private goods? When we are purchasing gifts and all supplies, we should firmly remember the two big words "National Products". Whether it is for eating, using, or wearing, whether it is for gifts or for self-use, no matter what, we should take purchasing national products as the standard. No matter how beautiful or cheap foreign goods are, we must stick to our principles and swear not to shake hands with them. Only in this way can our economic national crisis be resolved one day. Only in this way can the invasion of foreign goods and the rampant smuggling of private goods have the possibility of decline. This is a point that all fellow citizens across the country should deeply understand when purchasing gifts for the Mid-Autumn Festival.

Finally, the author has some additional opinions to offer. That is, when fellow citizens across the country are advocating national products with great enthusiasm, we should especially pay attention to the question of "Is this a national product?" when we give gifts to others. Because we are giving national products as gifts to others, on the one hand, we are respecting the other party, and at the same time, we are respecting ourselves. On the contrary, if we give imported goods to relatives and friends, it is no different from insulting the other person's personality, and at the same time, it is insulting our own personality. If you run into a very real friend, I am afraid they will return it to you intact and write a note to teach you a lesson. At that time, I ask: What fun is there in this?

Ladies who are busy purchasing gifts for the Mid-Autumn Festival, please carefully consider my opinions!

In the afternoon, they went to Taer Temple, 50 miles away from the city, and the Yang Tax Bureau in the mountains. On the way back to Xining, they also saw Lao You Bao Primary School and Fu Xian Bao Primary School. On the 22nd, they visited the Hui Muslim Promotion Association Senior High School, Central Elementary School, and First Elementary School in Xining in the morning. They also went to the Hui Muslim Promotion Association and visited the Da Qing Mosque. In the afternoon, they went to the Junior Industrial and Agricultural Vocational School and its affiliated elementary school, the Women's Simple Normal School and its affiliated elementary school, and the Qinghai Provincial Education Association, and visited the Sanitation Experiment Office. On the 23rd, Director Yang accompanied them to Tonghai Town, 90 miles away from the city, to see the Xining County Fifth Elementary School, the Northwest Epidemic Prevention Office, the Qinghai Veterinary Epidemic Prevention Institute, and the Xining Fourth District Livestock Conservation Association. On the way, they also saw the County Kang Le Township Elementary School. Also, Mr. Li and Mr. Bai accompanied the principal of Ledu Middle School to Ledu (120 miles away from Xining) on the 22nd to conduct inspections, and returned to Xining at noon on the 24th. On the morning of that day, Commissioner Guo inspected the An Quan Street Short-term Elementary School, the Xining Short-term Obligatory Women's Elementary School, the Min Heng Street Obligatory Elementary School, the County Nan Da Street Elementary School, the Nan Da Street Short-term Elementary School, and the Xining County Education Section. In the afternoon, Guo Mei and other five people went to An Quan Street Elementary School, the Provincial First Middle School, the Mongolian and Tibetan Culture Promotion Association and its affiliated Mongolian and Tibetan Elementary School, the Hainan Garrison Command Mongolian and Tibetan Elementary School, and the Qinghai Provincial Library. On the 25th, they went to the County Court Street Girls' Elementary School, the Provincial Mongolian Normal School, and the Xining Branch of the Central Political School. In the afternoon, they attended the Xining Primary and Secondary School Teachers' Welcome Meeting at the Provincial Government Auditorium. On the morning of the 26th, a large Eurasia aircraft flew to Xining at about 10:00 AM. Guo, Jiang, and Dai took this plane directly to Xi'an. Mr. Li continued his inspection of the provinces of Ningxia and Suiyuan via Lanzhou. The reporter went to the airport to see them off and asked Mr. Guo about his impressions of inspecting education in Qinghai. According to him, the educational administrators and teachers here are working hard for education in extremely meager conditions, which is commendable. He also praised the excellent achievements of the Xining County Calligraphy and Painting Labor Exhibition and, in the name of the group, presented a championship flag to the best senior elementary school and junior elementary school to mark the occasion. The reporter further inquired about how the British Boxer Indemnity Funds would be allocated after the completion of the inspection of the four provinces of Sui, Ning, and Gansu. He replied that he had consulted with the responsible authorities in each province during the inspection and that the recommendations would be submitted to the Board of Trustees for the Administration of the British Boxer Indemnity Funds in the near future. As for the fact that Mr. Guo was also ordered by the Ministry of Education to inspect the education in each province, he would also submit a detailed report to the Ministry separately.

City Museum's Opening Date Extended to October 15th

The Shanghai Municipal Museum in the city center was originally scheduled to officially open on October 1st, but due to the time required to decorate the interior display rooms, the project has not yet been completed and it will not be able to meet the public as scheduled. According to the person in charge of the museum, all the museum staff are working day and night to rush the layout and are expected to open on October 10th. However, because various models are complex, if they can't finish in time, the official opening will be no later than October 15th. In addition, the museum focuses on history and art, with history focusing on the history of Shanghai and art focusing on modern Chinese and world art. There are 48 general museums in China, and the layout and equipment of the Municipal Museum are among the best. It is said that after the opening, in order to limit the number of visitors, admission tickets will be sold, with adults paying one dime and children paying five cents. Ticket holders can visit the entire museum. School groups with official letters are exempt from fees.

Northeast Education Department Recommends Needy Students from the Northeast, Municipal Education Bureau Orders Compliance

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to public and registered private secondary schools stating: "According to the official letter from the Northeast Youth Education Relief Office of the Ministry of Education, regarding the Northeast Office's subsidy for needy students from the Northeast, in accordance with Item 6 of the 'Provisional Relief Measures for Needy Students from the Northeast' approved by the Executive Yuan and promulgated by the Ministry, the period for which subsidized students receive subsidies is one academic year, and the subsidy must be re-evaluated upon expiration. This has been the practice in the past. Now that the fifteenth year has begun, all students receiving subsidies for the twenty-fourth year will no longer be eligible for subsidies from this office as of the end of July of the twenty-fifth year. All old students from before the twenty-fourth year and new students from the twenty-fifth year should be re-examined by the school, and those who meet the provisions of the Northeast Office's 'Regulations for Subsidizing Needy Students from the Northeast' and are in genuine need of relief should be recommended to the office by the school they attend, in accordance with the subsidy regulations and with the attached recommendation deadline and instructions, for review and approval. In addition to separate letters, we are sending you the 'Regulations for Subsidizing Needy Students from the Northeast' and the application forms for recommendation, etc., for your reference and announcement, and to be forwarded to all subordinate public and registered private secondary schools (including county-level and private county-level middle schools; secondary schools affiliated with specialized schools and above are not included), ordering them to announce the aforementioned regulations, etc., and to conduct a thorough investigation of the needy students from the Northeast currently studying, and to proceed with the recommendation to the office in accordance with the procedures and the attached recommendation deadline and instructions, for review and approval." Attached are the 'Regulations for Subsidizing Needy Students from the Northeast,' the recommendation form, the recommendation roster, the attached table for recommendation names, and the recommendation deadline and instructions, etc., sent to the bureau. In addition to sending the attached documents, which are insufficient for distribution and will be kept at the bureau for collection, an order is hereby issued for compliance. This order."

Vocational Guidance Center Promotes Rabbit Farming as a Sideline

The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center has recently promoted rabbit farming as a sideline to improve people's livelihoods. Gan Chunquan, a staff member of the center, has compiled and printed a booklet, "Guidance on Rabbit Farming," based on his visits to rabbit farms in Japan and taking into account the situation in China, for reference when starting to farm various Chinese and foreign rabbit breeds. Anyone wishing to raise rabbits can send their address with two cents postage, and the center will send them a copy of "Guidance on Rabbit Farming" and its sequel. In addition, the "Mass Rural Sideline Monthly," edited by Gan, has been published to the third issue and contains articles on the production and sales of rabbits, actually promoting the rabbit farming business. With 20 cents postage, contact Gan at the center at No. 80 Hualong Road, Shanghai, to subscribe.
