Sports News

Municipal Education Bureau Announces Rules for Citywide Games, Registration Closed, Sign-up Begins Tomorrow, Those Who Have Not Registered Are Provisionally Allowed to Sign Up

The Fourth Citywide Games, sponsored by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, are scheduled to begin signing up at the Municipal Sports Ground from tomorrow until the 11th. The registration for each school's participating events closed on the 28th. For those schools that have not yet registered but still request to participate, the Education Bureau, in order to promote physical education, will provisionally allow them to sign up. The rules of the Games have been submitted to the municipal government for approval and have been officially announced. They are recorded as follows:

Eligibility: Article 1. This conference is sponsored by the Municipal Education Bureau with the aim of popularizing civic sports and promoting sports in schools at all levels throughout the city. Article 2. This conference will be held in four groups: Open, College, Middle School, and Sports School. Except for the Open Group, which is based on individuals, the other groups are based on schools. The eligibility requirements are as follows: (1) Open Group: Any citizen currently residing within the city limits, with a male age of 18 or older and a female age of 16 or older, in good health, with proper conduct, and not violating the qualifications and spirit of amateur sports, can participate. (2) College Group: All currently enrolled students in public and private colleges and universities (excluding sports colleges) in the city can participate, based on schools. (3) Middle School Group: All currently enrolled students in municipal public schools and registered or approved private secondary schools in the city can participate, based on schools, divided into senior high and junior high sections. (4) Sports School Group: All currently enrolled students in sports schools at all levels in the city or in university sports departments can participate, based on schools, divided into specialized and normal sections. Article 3. This conference will be held at the sports ground in the city center. Article 4. The opening date of this conference is three days, from October 22nd to October 24th, 25th year, which may be changed by the president of this conference when necessary. Article 5.

Conference Organization: This conference will have one honorary president, who will be the mayor. Article 6. This conference will have one president, who will be the director of the Education Bureau, and two vice-presidents, who will be the head of the responsible section, to preside over all conference affairs. Article 7. This conference will have one secretary-general, who will be the supervisor in charge of physical education, to handle the conference's routine affairs under the orders of the president. Article 8. For the convenience of handling affairs, this conference will be divided into two departments: administrative and competitive. Each department will have one director. The administrative department will have six sections: documentation, accounting, general affairs, reception, security, and sanitation. The competitive department will have five sections: venue equipment, registration, allocation, referees, records, and prizes. Each section will have one chief and one deputy chief, and several staff members, all of whom will be appointed by the director of the Education Bureau. They will all be unpaid positions. Article 9. This conference will have a qualification review committee to review the qualifications of participating athletes. Its members will be appointed by the director of the Education Bureau. Article 10. This conference will have a judging committee to adjudicate all disputes over sports matters during the conference. Its members will be appointed by the director of the Education Bureau.

Sports Events: Article 11. Sports are divided into three sections: group exercises, track and field, and traditional Chinese martial arts. The items are as follows: (A) Group Exercise Section: (1) General Assembly Exercise: Based on schools, the number of participants from each school will be designated by the Education Bureau. If a school has not been designated but wishes to participate, each unit will consist of 50 people. (3) Group exercises, such as traditional Chinese martial arts, marching, calisthenics, game equipment, fitness dance, etc., divided into senior high and junior high sections. Note: General Assembly Exercises and group exercises are limited to middle school and physical education normal school students. (B) Track and Field Section: (1) Open Group: (A) Men's: Field Events: High Jump, Pole Vault, Long Jump, Triple Jump, Shot Put (16 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw; Track Events: 100m, 200m, 400m, 800m, 1500m, 10000m, 110m Hurdles, 400m Hurdles, Pentathlon, Decathlon. (B) Women's: Track and Field: High Jump, Long Jump, Shot Put (8 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw, Softball Throw (12 inch), 50m, 100m, 200m, 80m Hurdles. (2) College Group: (A) Men's: Field Events: High Jump, Long Jump, Pole Vault, Triple Jump, Shot Put (16 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw; Track Events: 100m, 200m, 400m, 800m, 1500m, 10000m, 110m Hurdles, 400m Hurdles, Pentathlon, Decathlon, 4x100m Relay, 4x400m Relay. (B) Women's: Track and Field: High Jump, Long Jump, Shot Put (8 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw, Softball Throw (12 inch), 50m, 100m, 200m, 80m Hurdles, 4x100m Relay. (3) Middle School Group: (A) Senior High Men's: Field Events: High Jump, Pole Vault, Long Jump, Triple Jump, Shot Put (12 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw; Track Events: 100m, 200m, 400m, 800m, 1500m, 5000m, 110m Hurdles, 400m Hurdles, 4x100m Relay, 4x400m Relay. (B) Senior High Women's: Track and Field: High Jump, Long Jump, Javelin Throw, Discus Throw, Softball Throw (12 inch), Shot Put (8 lbs), 50m, 100m, 200m, 80m Hurdles, 4x100m Relay. (C) Junior High Men's: Field Events: High Jump, Pole Vault, Long Jump, Triple Jump, Shot Put (8 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw; Track Events: 100m, 200m, 400m, 800m, 1500m, 200m Hurdles, 4x100m Relay, 4x200m Relay. (D) Junior High Women's: Track and Field: High Jump, Long Jump, Javelin Throw, Softball Throw (12 inch), Shot Put (6 lbs), 50m, 100m, 200m, 80m Hurdles, 4x50m Relay. (4) Sports School Group: (A) Specialized Men's: Field Events: High Jump, Pole Vault, Long Jump, Triple Jump, Shot Put (16 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw; Track Events: 100m, 200m, 400m, 800m, 1500m, 10000m, 110m Hurdles, 400m Hurdles, Pentathlon, Decathlon, 4x100m Relay, 4x400m Relay. (B) Specialized Women's: Track and Field: High Jump, Long Jump, Shot Put (8 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw, Softball Throw (12 inch), 50m, 100m, 200m, 400m, 80m Hurdles, 4x100m Relay. (C) Normal School Men's: Field Events: High Jump, Pole Vault, Long Jump, Triple Jump, Shot Put (16 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw; Track Events: 100m, 200m, 400m, 800m, 1500m, 10000m, 110m Hurdles, 400m Hurdles, Pentathlon, Decathlon, 4x100m Relay, 4x400m Relay. (D) Normal School Women's: Track and Field: High Jump, Long Jump, Shot Put (8 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw, Softball Throw (12 inch), 50m, 100m, 200m, 400m, 80m Hurdles, 4x100m Relay. (C) Traditional Chinese Martial Arts Section: Based on individuals, divided into performance and competition groups. (1) Performance Group: Divided into men's and women's boxing and weapons. (2) Competition Group: Divided into men's and women's wrestling, archery, slingshot, and weightlifting.

Championships and Awards: Article 12. In track and field events, each athlete can register for a maximum of four events, excluding relay races. In the Open, College, and Sports School Groups, men and women are limited to four events. In the Middle School Group, men and women are limited to three events. In the College, Middle School, and Sports School Groups, each school is limited to four people per event per group. Four places will be recorded for each event, and the scores will be calculated as 5, 3, 2, 1. In traditional Chinese martial arts competitions, each person is limited to four events. Four places will be recorded for each event, and the scores will be calculated as 5, 3, 2, 1. (No championship will be awarded. No scores will be given for traditional Chinese martial arts performances, but awards will be given to outstanding performers. Article 13. In this track and field team championship, except for the Open Group, which will not have one, the College, Middle School, and Sports School Groups will each have men's and women's championships. The unit with the most points will win the championship, and the three units with the next highest scores will win the runner-up, third, and fourth places. If two or more units have the same score, the unit with the most first-place finishes in each event will be judged to have won. The rest can be inferred by analogy. Article 14. Athletes in the track and field Open Group and the traditional Chinese martial arts competition group who achieve special results will be given certificates to encourage them. Article 15. Middle school group exercise teams with excellent results will be given certificates. Article 16. The rules of the competition will be based on the rules of the 6th National Games and the All-China Athletic Association. Article 17. These rules will be implemented after being submitted to the municipal government for record and promulgation.

Records of the World Games Delegation's Journey - Letter 16 - Special Correspondent Feng Youzhen from the Central News Agency

The Chinese delegation participating in the Games, with the exception of the soccer team which, upon invitation, left Berlin on the 12th to compete in Frankfort, and then to compete in countries such as Austria, England, and France; the members of the sports inspection team also departed Germany on the evening of the second day after the closing ceremony, at 10 p.m., to inspect Austria, Finland, Denmark, and other countries. The remaining athletes stayed in Berlin. On the 17th, the Chinese Ambassador to Germany, Cheng Dafang, hosted a farewell banquet at the Blau-Weiss Tennis Club. On the 18th, the General Association of Chinese Students in Europe held the opening ceremony of its second annual meeting in Bad Saarow (65 kilometers from Berlin), in the eastern suburbs of Berlin. All the athletes attended, and the basketball and swimming athletes also participated in demonstrations. President Dai hosted a lunch banquet for all the athletes. That evening, they returned to the Olympic Village, and the hospitality ended on the 18th. The male and female athletes moved into the city and stayed in hotels separately. From the 24th to the 26th, they were divided into groups to visit the National Socialist Party, military, youth organizations, volunteer labor teams, labor organizations, well-known municipal factories, national motorways, and social relief undertakings. From the 29th, they were free to act independently. On the night of September 1st, at 9:13 p.m., they departed Germany in a special train carriage from Berlin, passing through Austria to Italy. Approximately a hundred German government representatives and students studying abroad came to the station to see them off. It is expected that they will arrive in Naples on the morning of the 3rd and embark on the Conte Rosso liner on the 4th, and will be able to return to their motherland around the end of the month.

Government representative President Dai, due to other tasks, could not accompany the delegation. He is scheduled to travel by ship from France in mid-September to return to Kyoto before the Double Ten Festival. Head of Delegation Wang Zhengting will travel to the Soviet Union, Poland, Austria, and other countries for a short period of inspection. He is scheduled to return home on the same ship as the delegation on the 4th in Naples. Secretary-General Shen Siliang had already departed on August 21st via Siberia due to personal matters. Head Coach Ma John and Basketball Coach Dong Shouyi will remain in Berlin and are scheduled to inspect sports in various European countries and the United States. Their return to China is expected to be a year later. Jiang Lianggui and Luan Xianqu, members of the sports inspection team, and athlete Jia Lianren will remain in Germany to study sports. The reporter, due to visiting European news organizations, also intends to stay for several months. The "Records of the Journey" hereby comes to an end. If anything is gained from the European trip, I will report to the readers again separately.

(7) (7) Annual Meeting of the General Association of Chinese Students in Europe

Before ending the "Records of the Journey," a detailed report on the situation of the second annual meeting of the "General Association of Chinese Students in Europe" should be made to the readers, because the students in Europe have helped the delegation a lot this time. It can be said that they are an important member of the delegation's expedition. Furthermore, the situation of the students studying abroad must also be of concern to the readers.

History of the General Association of Students

The history of China sending young students to study abroad is as long as that of Japan. The efforts of Japanese students completed the great task of the Meiji Restoration, and now they are famous all over the world. Although Chinese students have also made many contributions to the motherland, they cannot be compared with Japan, and they are far from the expectations of the Chinese people. The reasons are roughly two points: First, there is no close connection between the government and the students studying abroad. Often the government needs talents but cannot find them. At the same time, students with specialized knowledge often do not have the opportunity to contribute their talents after returning to China, forming a contradictory phenomenon. Second, the factions among students studying abroad are divided, and the concept of "family" is very deep. Not only can they not cooperate, but they also exclude each other. If we want to make the students studying abroad truly contribute to the country, we must eliminate these two defects, otherwise there is no hope forever. Students studying in various European countries have student organizations in many countries. In recent years, they feel that it is necessary to expand these small organizations and to melt the emotions and knowledge of students studying abroad in the whole of Europe. Initiated by the student associations of England, France, and the Netherlands, the inaugural meeting of the "General Association of Chinese Students in Europe" was held in London in August 1934. The charter was adopted, stipulating that an annual meeting should be held once during the summer vacation each year. The first annual meeting was held in Amsterdam, the capital of the Netherlands, in August 1935. This year, due to the convenience of the World Games, the second annual meeting was held in Germany. In addition to the representatives of England, Germany, and the Netherlands, students from Italy and Austria also officially sent representatives to attend. The remaining countries, such as France, Belgium, Switzerland, and Poland, only had informal representatives present because they did not yet have student organizations. In addition, there were a total of 150 to 160 students from various countries participating. The third annual meeting is scheduled to be held in London in August next year. It is expected that all countries will have official representatives to attend, so that the organization of the General Association will become more sound.

Representatives of this Annual Meeting

Double Coin Cup Summer Football Finale Champions China Aviation Runners-up Jiangnan

The local Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory has always been enthusiastic about promoting sports. This summer, it specially launched the Double Coin Cup Summer Football Tournament. More than ten teams participated. None of the participating teams forfeited or withdrew. The weather this summer was hot, but they still persevered. The good sportsmanship can be said to have set a new record. The day before yesterday was the final. The teams that won the right to the final were China Aviation and Jiangnan Shipyard. The referee Shen Huichun blew the whistle at 8 am. The skills of both sides can be said to be comparable. The battle was full of highlights. Neither side scored in the first half. In the second half, the two sides held each other until the 20th minute, when China Aviation center Wu Guozhi scored a goal with a long shot. After that, Jiangnan tried its best to counterattack, hovering in front of the China Aviation goal many times. Unfortunately, due to inaccurate shooting, they did not score. As a result, China Aviation won 1-0 over Jiangnan. Afterwards, the Double Coin Cup consolation final was held. The teams that won the right to the final were Hengda and Overseas Chinese. Lu Shunde was the referee. Hengda fought bravely and opened the scoring first, but Overseas Chinese had a stronger strength. As a result, Overseas Chinese won 4-2 over Hengda.

Western Police Football Team Actually Opposes Holding Games at the City Sports Field Yesterday's Letter to the League Committee Explains the Reasons

Guoguang News Agency reported that the City Sports Field was specially built by the city government last year for the 6th National Games. The equipment is perfect and is the only large sports field in the Far East. Recently, the Donghua Football Club, because the environment is suitable, specially negotiated to borrow the field as their home field for the Western League games. The competition authorities have agreed. The trial match against Portugal the previous week and the official match against St. Francis last week were both held at the field. This week's match against the Western Police was held at Yiyuan because the Western Police was the home team. Unexpectedly, the Western Police team suddenly sent a letter to the League Committee the night before, expressing their opposition to holding future games at the City Sports Field. The reason is that the situation there is special, the transportation is inconvenient, and it is not suitable for football games. After receiving the letter, the committee has not yet convened a meeting to discuss it or replied to the team. According to the Western Police team, the annual rent for the second field of the Racecourse as their home field is 600 yuan. The rent for this year (1936-7) could not be paid due to economic difficulties. A meeting was held at the team's clubhouse on Fuzhou Road the night before (28th), but no concrete solution was reached.

Cotton Yarn Prices are Expected to Rise Cotton Yarn Market is Booming Yarn Rises by Two or Three Yuan Cotton Rises by Seven or Eight Jiao

The yarn market rose sharply in the morning, then fell back in the afternoon. However, the actual sales have been active in recent days, and the cash withdrawals from various parties are particularly strong, which is exciting. The short sellers are eager to cover their positions, and the market is showing a soaring trend. The October and November contracts broke through the 210 yuan mark. In the afternoon, the market was shrouded in unfavorable atmosphere, and the long positions took profits, causing the market price to fall back by 9 jiao to 1.2 yuan.

(Spot Yarn Rises in the Morning and Falls Back in the Afternoon)

The spot yarn market opened in the morning due to the settlement of the previous day, the situation of spot yarn and the rise in overseas cotton industry, the market sentiment was excited, and buyers gathered in the market as soon as the market opened. The short sellers, seeing the active sales of yarn, were eager to cover their positions, and each month rose by 2.5 to 3.5 yuan. The second session fell slightly, and by the third closing, it was still firm in the near term. The thinking of the industry was bullish, reaching a boiling point. The market trading was extremely prosperous. The market closed at 1:00 pm. The market extended to 3:00 pm in the afternoon, but some of the industry found that the price had risen by 18 yuan compared with the price on September 2. For the long positions, it was temporarily abandoned. It was found that Mingde, Gengfeng, Taichang, Changfeng, Xincheng, and Jinkang unanimously sold out, while Tongji, Shenji, Dachang, Fukang, and Jinchang tried hard to buy in. As a result, each month rose by 2.8 to 3.6 jiao compared with the closing price of the previous day, and October rose by 4.3 jiao. The market situation turned flat in the afternoon. Due to profit-taking, the market also reported unfavorable environment, and the selling trend became stronger, and the market fell step by step. As a result, each month fell by 9 jiao to 1.2 yuan compared with the closing price in the morning. It was found that Gengfeng sold 11,600 bales, Mingde 3,700 bales, Yukang 1,300 bales, Fengtai 1,900 bales, Taichang 2,500 bales, Changfeng 5,000 bales, Xinhua 1,750 bales, Jinkang 2,350 bales, Hexing 2,150 bales, and Changyu 1,800 bales. Tongji bought 4,900 bales, Yuda 2,800 bales, Jifeng 1,050 bales, Deda 1,750 bales, Yuanda 1,900 bales, Jinchang 1,800 bales, Shenji 9,650 bales, Renfeng 1,650 bales, Dachang 4,300 bales, Tonghe 1,500 bales, and Fukang 1,650 bales. However, there were too many short positions in the October contract, so the recent trend turned upward. Special Certificate Fees Will Be Added to Cotton Yarn Starting Next Month

Yarn Fee 8 Yuan Cotton Fee 3 Yuan

The Yarn and Cloth Exchange will collect a special certificate cash of 8 yuan per bale for new transactions of the previous month's cotton yarn starting from the 1st, and a special certificate cash of 3 yuan per dan for new transactions of October cotton. Complete Change of Standards for March Futures Yarn

The Chinese Yarn Market Exchange convened a yarn and cotton appraisal meeting on September 15th to review the substitute grades for the standard yarn and cotton of the March 1937 futures. The result of the review was a complete change in the grades of coarse and fine yarns, but the cotton grades for March remained unchanged, the same as in February. The changes are listed below:

(1) Equivalent products: Hongfu, Double Earth, Three Sheep, and Golden Pagoda brands are all raised to equivalent products.

(2) 20-count Red Kui Xing, Weaver Girl, Double Deer, Three Stars, Golden City, Single Earth, Ball Crane, Big Airship, and Rainbow Kui Xing, a total of nine brands, remain the same as the February grades. All other brands are increased by one yuan.

(3) All brands of 16-count yarn are increased by one yuan.

(4) All brands of 10-count yarn are increased by two yuan.

General Buying Sentiment at US Cotton Close

Yesterday, US cotton opened with increases of 10 to 12 points per pound for all months. In the early morning, news from Liverpool was good, and interpretations of international finance favored buyers. There was heavy rain and cold weather in the western cotton regions. Foreign merchants bought in, and the market was very firm. Later, long positions were closed and cotton merchants sold short, resulting in a slight softening. New off-market participants were discovered. Although the rain in the west was sufficient to hinder cotton picking and damage the quality of cotton, buyers were still concerned. Before the close, private reports indicated damage to new cotton in Texas. Cloth sales were active, and the public bought in, pushing prices up again. The close was firm, with spot prices up 13 points per pound and futures up 9 to 14 points per pound. British cotton spot prices were up 6 points and futures up 4 points. Indian cotton European exporters absorbed the outflow from long positions, but later retreated due to profit-taking by long positions. Bengal rose by 1 rupee, Oomra rose by half a rupee, and White Broach rose by 0.75 rupee. The original telegram is recorded on the left (dated 28th).

Three Grades of Yarn and Cotton Continue to Rise According to an Osaka telegram on the 29th, three grades of yarn futures rose by 80 sen to falling by 10 sen. The near month was 212.90 yuan, and the far month was 206.20 yuan. Cotton futures rose by 10 sen to 35 sen. The near month was 66.20 yuan, and the far month was 65.65 yuan.

Piece Goods and Cotton Cloth Rise Strongly

In recent days, the cloth market has been greatly influenced by the soaring prices of yarn, the devaluation of the French franc, and the unanimous surge in the global cotton market, resulting in increasingly enthusiastic sentiment. Cloth prices have risen sharply, with some rising by 30 to 40 sen per piece in a single day. Various factories have raised their asking prices, with white goods rising by another 10 sen per piece and printed, dyed, and finished goods rising by another 15 to 45 sen per piece. Only bleached cloth is selling poorly due to the off-season. Hengfeng's Chenghua Splash Velvet, originally sold at 18.5 sen per yard, is now quoted at 19.5 sen. Guangzhong's Pine Crane Middle Pattern Velvet has increased from 18 sen last week to 19 sen and is now priced at 20 sen. Meiheng Factory's Qi Jiguang Mass Serge, Thrift Serge, and Big Crepe Serge, originally sold at 30 to 35 sen, have also increased in price by 15 to 30 sen per piece. Internal and external factories' Four Gentlemen Serge and Direct Tribute have also increased by 15 sen per piece. Other factories' patterned goods have also risen sharply. White goods, especially lightweight coarse cloth, are in the best position due to the current shortage on the market. Various purchasing agents continue to buy, and although market prices are high, the intention to purchase does not decrease. Cotton cloth sales at various factories and stores are booming, and business has more than doubled. Yesterday, due to border controls, shipments of goods for inland buyers were slightly reduced. Merchant buyers still shipped out some spot goods.

Finance: Although Pure Gold Surges Violently, Standard Gold is Not Stimulated; Day's Trading Initially Weak, Then Stable, Resulting in a Decline of 3.9 Yuan

Gold Market: Although pure gold soared and exchange rates shrank sharply, people were still not satisfied, and the market immediately fell back upon opening. Midway through, due to infighting among Chinese and foreign speculators, it was still easy to pull up. In the early morning, the overseas silver market saw British prices rise and American prices remain stable. Deferred silver prices in Montreux rose by 2.7 to 7.7 points. The exchange rate of British currency against plummeted by 9.625 points, and the exchange rate of British currency against French currency was still difficult to open. The exchange rate of American currency against British currency continued to fall by 2.375 points, while the exchange rate of American currency against French currency rose by 15 sen. The price of raw gold in London soared by 2 shillings and 11.5 pence, but people were still not satisfied. The off-market pre-market trading opened and immediately fell to 58.9 yuan. Fuxing, Yongqing, Fayong, Qiafeng, Yongyuan, and Mao Yong sold strips, falling to 52 yuan. Chunyuan, Yongfuxing, Yongheng, Yushun, and Maolaijin. The Central Bank's price was announced, with British and American currencies both flat and the customs gold unit rising by 2.6 sen. The standard gold price was listed at 1144.6 yuan, rising to above 55 yuan. The morning opened with a low price. After the opening, major players swarmed in, but also took the opportunity to sell at high prices. Therefore, although prices rose, there were many transactions, and the supply and demand were evenly matched, resulting in a very stable overall trend. The HSBC Bank's price was announced, with British and American currencies both flat. The market began to stabilize. Midway through, there was a decline, but buying sentiment remained strong. Later, the silver equalization tax rose by 1.75 sen, and short sellers also covered, breaking through the 60 yuan mark. Short sellers took the opportunity to exert pressure, and the market soon rebounded slightly, gradually leveling off. Although the market was flat in the afternoon, major short sellers came to cover, and buying sentiment was strong again, gradually improving. However, the upward trend was blocked by those who went long and short, and the deferred contract rose to 4.8 yuan yesterday. The daily market conditions are recorded below.

The morning opening was 1154.5 yuan, 7.2 yuan lower than the previous close. Dadecheng, Dafeng, Hengchun, Chunyuan, Yongyuan, and Mao Yong purchased strips, rising to 6.5 yuan. Dadecheng and Yuxinxiang sold, falling to 5.3 yuan. Fuda, Fuxing, Yongyuan, and Mao Yong continued to rise to 7.5 yuan. Fuxing, Yongyuan, Mao Yong, Hengchang, Yongqian, Changxiang sold. Grain: Flour Delivery Does Not Wait Until Expiration

Yesterday was the delivery date for September flour futures, but there was no formal fulfillment on the exchange. Because the delivery was changed to public warehouses, the procedures were inconvenient and the costs were secretly increased. Therefore, both counterparties, such as customers, contacted the factory early if they wanted to withdraw the goods. Conversely, if the factory had a surplus that had not been settled, the brokers involved also peddled it to customers. Therefore, under the current situation, formal delivery is only carried out when absolutely necessary.

Considerable Number of Coarse Grains Delivered

Yesterday's coarse grain trading saw a total of 26 carloads of wheat delivered throughout the day, with number 4 delivering 6 carloads, number 5 delivering 1 carload, number 6 delivering 2 carloads, number 10 delivering 2 carloads, number 12 delivering 3 carloads, number 16 delivering 1 carload, number 26 delivering 3 carloads, number 27 delivering 2 carloads, and number 38 delivering 6 carloads. The delivery of standard oil was also quite active, with number 6 delivering 4,400 loads and number delivering ... The Hakka Coarse Indica Rice and Cantonese Group Continue to be Actively Traded

Yesterday, the market conditions for Hakka indica rice were robust in both arrival and sales, with an excellent market atmosphere. In particular, coarse indica rice was actively traded by the Cantonese group, and with limited inventory, the market continued to see a slight increase in prices. Yesterday, the Cantonese group purchased seven to eight thousand bags of coarse rice from various sources, with prices increasing by about one and a half jiao compared to the previous market. Other mills were actively traded by this street and the Shantou group, and market prices also showed a slight increase. The overall market opened with 6,850 bags of Jiangxi rice, 5,350 bags of Hunan rice, 300 bags of Nanjing coarse rice, and 3,500 bags of Hubei coarse rice.

Mid-Autumn Festival Arrives, Rice Sales Stagnate

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the total arrival from various groups was around 18 or 19, with a total of nearly 4,000 shi of goods. The West Street sales market remained sluggish due to the approaching festival. Therefore, new thin rice varieties such as Baige Yao and others, although there were more than 300 bags purchased by the Qingdao and Dalian groups, the resulting market prices decreased by a small one jiao to one and a half jiao. The price of thick new japonica rice also fell by one jiao. New sharp varieties like Du Yang and others continued to be scarce, and the market atmosphere remained stable. Broken and thick grains remained unchanged. The Qingdao group only purchased a few hundred bags of thin rice, and the market showed a trend of stability with a hint of softness. There was no supply of old rice that had turned into yuan. The supply of new rice that had turned into yuan exceeded demand, and prices fell by about one jiao.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, more than 20 shipments arrived from various groups downstream. The market sales of various goods, including broken japonica, mutated yuan, old thin rice, were dull. Western new japonica, new Yang Du埠 Hakka sharp rice were quite good. Market prices for broken japonica, mutated yuan, old thin rice, were sluggish by a few fen to nearly one jiao. New japonica, new Yang Du埠 Hakka sharp rice were tight by several fen. Eastern new japonica was stable, while Yao varieties were sluggish. Baige fell by a small one jiao. Today is the Mid-Autumn Festival, and according to regulations, the rice industry in both the north and south markets will suspend measuring for one day.

Silk and Tea Domestic Silk Market Feels Even More Quiet

Yesterday, the New York silk market and the price of Chinese and Japanese raw silk both tended to soften. Except for Guangdong silk, each fell by one point. In exchange trading, the near-term was 12 and a half, and the far-term months remained unchanged. The market, however, was stalled due to many clean and soft silks, and there were no transactions in raw silk. There were no market quotes yesterday. Yokohama spot futures rose slightly by six to nine yuan, and were seen to be firm again in the afternoon. However, the local silk market felt quiet, and foreign firms also gradually ceased operations. Domestic users and hoarders also reduced their activity due to the uncertain situation. The total silk transaction for the whole day was only 56 bales. Today is the Mid-Autumn Festival, and foreign merchants are also taking a customary holiday, so the domestic silk market may feel even more quiet.

Needle-Shaped Green Tea Sales Are Also Strong

Yesterday, the green tea market of foreign firms continued to be buoyant. Zhejiang Pingshui tea and Lüzhuang Zhenmei green tea were first promoted by Jardine Matheson & Co., and other firms followed suit one after another. Even the Xiehe Foreign Firm for needle-shaped green tea also absorbed a large quantity. The total transaction volume of green tea in the city was more than 3,200 boxes, and the selling prices tended to be stable. As for the black tea market, the Shanghai market is about to end. It is heard that foreign firms are still planning to go to Henan and Hubei to continue their operations.

According to reports from tea warehouses, the green tea market has been affected by the devaluation of the French franc. Telegrams sent to Morocco a few days ago have not been responded to, so the market is very quiet. However, the Pingshui Zhenmei and Lüzhuang Xiumei that were previously discussed by various firms were officially traded yesterday. It is feared that the market will be difficult to develop for a while due to the French franc.

Spring and Autumn

Mid-Autumn Musings

— (Shufan)

White water and green reeds, a misty sorrow, not related to Qu Yuan lamenting on the riverbank. The sound of insects is clear and the merchant ships are steady, a row of cool lanterns moored for the passing of autumn!

Making a living by wandering the rivers and lakes, most fearful of the Mid-Autumn Festival. What can a traveler do tonight to dispel this feeling? A poem forms with disappointment, almost unbearable. Thirty years of life, considering its prime, is like the midpoint of autumn, the moon nearing its fullness. To dedicate oneself to society and country, it wouldn't be without some benefit. However, every step encounters obstacles, unable to reach the important path, leading to days and nights spent circling between wine cups and rice bowls, as if fearing falling behind. Year after year, the moon is bright, and I remain the same. Why must Huan Sima stroke the autumn willow to feel sentimental?

The azure sky shines with purity, but floating clouds invade, causing immediate alarm. No wonder Qu Yuan by the lakeside was alone and awake amidst the drunken masses. Therefore, the moon is intentionally bright, but the clouds are merciless. Applying this to people, wanting to move the vulgar with pure and impartial conduct, is it not difficult? What's gratifying is that the cool wind blows away the clouds, and clarity still remains. The darkness and changes do not harm the moon. This is why those with unique and independent spirits are bright and upright, enduring obstacles without regret? During this Mid-Autumn Festival, I suddenly contemplate my own position.

The moon is exceptionally bright during Mid-Autumn. This is why Mao Pijiang considered it the purest and most secluded time. Pijiang was merely afraid that the moonlight and autumn dew wouldn't last long. But for those who find inspiration in people and scenery, the feelings are different. Some families are joyful, some are sorrowful—this is the sentiment of children. Cool lanterns and flying dreams—how is the autumn frontier guard doing? This is what the valiant feel. "Pitying one's swaying shadow beneath the tree, who repaints the thousand-yuan heads of people?" This is the hero wanting to tread the battlefield but lacking a path. This year, tonight, who has the most autumn thoughts? Look at the waving clouds, how will each understand it!

Going to the Moon

— Qingqu

The moon is also one of the planets; therefore, it is a whole entity, not a fabricated illusion. Why is its light exceptionally bright during mid-autumn? Because the moon also has waxing and waning phases, and it meets the sun twice a month on the same meridian. The time between these meetings is called "new moon and full moon," approximately 29 days, 12 hours, 44 minutes, and 2.87 seconds. Since the apparent diameter varies, and its orbit is elliptical, the moon appears to people as a hook or a half-wheel, gradually becoming like a bright mirror. Throughout the year, no moon is brighter than tonight's. Traditionally, people on this Mid-Autumn night compete to admire the beautiful moonlight. However, the so-called traveling to the moon palace and bowing to Chang'e is absurd and has no effect, which goes without saying. Therefore, I say that science is advancing rapidly, and humans will one day reach the moon, which is a foregone conclusion.

Consider the earlier announcement by the American technician Kong Zhao of "traveling to Venus," and the later invention of rockets by Dr. Weiba Nahaofu, with the "news of corresponding with the moon." Recently, there was the British Dr. Lopison who "directly called Mars via radio." Judging by these examples, the moon is not too far from Earth. Compared to today's around-the-world travelers, the distance they travel exceeds the time and distance from Earth to the Moon. Then, will An He and others jointly tour the moon palace? Some say, "Impossible, no matter what! Once we reach the highest altitude, there is an obstacle, that is, the lack of breathable air, which will inevitably cause suffocation." Can one still ascend? "I say, don't worry," haven't you heard that chemists can create air? Along the way, when reaching the vacuum, clean air can be fully loaded and carried along. If so, why worry about not being able to visit the moon to conduct on-site experiments?

People today only know to worship and admire the moon. I say it's better to emulate the research of scientists, perhaps explore, perhaps travel, which is better than being confined to the tiny Earth, preventing people from moving forward. Moreover, speaking of launching rockets, it is said that "it is as convenient and direct as a mailbag. Like Vienna to New Zealand, it only takes 56 minutes. To reach the moon, the elapsed time, at most, is only one week, and the destination can be reached." Some say, "This is your dream." I say, please look at the aviation in the sky, what is it like now? Didn't the Western philosopher Vilin also say that flying machines were a fool's fantasy? But who would have thought that today it has become a world of aviation? Therefore, I believe that in the future, we will surely realize this statement, competing to go to the moon one day. Alas, those who burn incense and only know to look at the moon, wasting this fine night, are truly foolish.

The moon is exceptionally bright during Mid-Autumn

—

Autumn Insects, Autumn Moon

— Rongyu

The swimming pool no longer has those fashionable men and women frolicking in the water; the cold drink shop has also taken down its sign, changing to a different business. On the pedestrian sidewalk, one no longer sees the poor sleeping in the open at night. All these scenes have hinted to people that autumn has arrived. Autumn is solemn and austere, autumn is lonely. Many poets and writers are sighing and chanting, creating many moving poems and prose. In fact, autumn never makes people lonely, nor does it harm a single hair on their heads. Saying that autumn is bitter and boring is truly complaining without illness. If you don't believe it, look at the many leisure classes and many bourgeois, who are greatly enjoying their autumn insects and savoring their autumn moon!

Indeed, there are many insects in autumn, such as crickets, katydids, and bell crickets. Whenever the night is deep and still, when dew drips and coldness invades, they chirp and sing loudly in the steps of the courtyard, under the bean trellises and melon frames, making many people feel unhappy. However, besides singing loudly, crickets also open their teeth and fight each other, making them practitioners of militarism, thus they are played with by people, becoming representatives of autumn insects. People raise them in earthenware pots, feeding them rice grains, seeming to cherish them to the utmost; but in fact, they are using their strength to win their own prize. Dressed in armor and displaying their power, they are nothing more than small puppets.

The autumn sky is high and clear, and the moon in the evening seems particularly bright. Because of the love of admiring the bright moon, the invention of mooncakes came about. Using the example of "Six Writings," this also belongs to the "associative compounds" category. The origin of mooncakes cannot be traced, but according to folk tales, at the end of the Yuan dynasty, the families of the Han people were monitored by Tartars - Mongols. At that time, Liu Bowen, holding racial revolutionary thoughts, bribed cake shops to insert paper slips inside the cakes, writing, "We Han people, quickly rise up and kill all the Tartars." Therefore, there is the story of eating mooncakes to kill Tartars, showing that mooncakes have been around for a long time. However, people nowadays are not as foolish as the ancients; and in this time of advocating good neighborliness, even if you have ten thousand grievances, you have to swallow them, so you chew the mooncakes without discerning whether the taste is sour, spicy, bitter, or sweet.

The moon is exceptionally bright during Mid-Autumn

— Yafei

Ten years ago, on a certain Mid-Autumn night, I was drifting in a certain city, living a desolate and lonely wandering life. In a small building, I was writing line after line on manuscript paper. The room was as quiet as death. Besides the sound of the pen tip scratching on the manuscript paper, one could not hear any other sound around.

Although it was a city, because I lived on the outskirts, the environment was very quiet. Especially at night, all sounds and activities gradually subsided. The flame of the electric lamp slowly faded, and I seemed to feel a bit tired, but I just couldn't sleep. The surrounding tranquility gave me a terrible threat, making me lack the courage to sit any longer. So I turned off the lamp and threw my body onto the bed.

Mid-Autumn is a good festival in the year. Some refined people who enjoy admiring the moon, of course, have not missed this fine day and beautiful scenery. But I, "raising my head to look at the bright moon, lower my head and think of my hometown"; in such a full moon season, I am still drifting alone in a foreign land, just watching helplessly as this ungraspable time steals away from the shadows of my life. "On every festive occasion, I think even more of my relatives," and thinking of this, I can't help but sadly shed tears.

I suddenly got up from the bed, pushed open the window, and only saw a bright expanse of moonlight; however, a kind of sorrow had gently climbed into my consciousness, making me feel as if I had a belly of grievances to pour out to the bright moonlight.

On the writing desk, I laid out a sheet of manuscript paper, dipped the pen tip full of ink, and, with the help of the moonlight, wanted to write something; but, but what should I write about?

Suddenly, up to now, several more lonely Mid-Autumn nights have passed in the years of that wandering life. However, I drifted from this city to that city; over the years, I have only been busy with worldly affairs, and my hardworking life has not allowed me to stay properly in one place. Moreover, the famine of unemployment has pushed me onto this long-forgotten old road!

Autumn has quietly passed by half way. The Mid-Autumn Festival that people rejoice and dance for is coming. However, in this day when the country has reached the point of mountains and rivers being broken, and society is in the midst of a panic about livelihood, I can't help but be educated to be moved by the scene and feel sorrow at the moon, and once again "sadly shed tears"!

Now when I see mooncakes, I am reminded of our country; because our country now, in the eyes of the great powers, is simply a mooncake, and they can come to bite it or divide a piece at will, digging out the filling and peeling off the skin, wanting to eat it all up before stopping. The moon may be the same brightness every year, the same reunion, and those who enjoy admiring the moon will certainly not decrease, but what about our country's territory? Ah! Country, society, self... I really dare not think about them anymore.

"On the fifteenth day of the eighth month, the moon is bright..." I will still sing a "back" to vent this pent-up anger in my heart!

Examination of Elegant Names for the Moon

As the Mid-Autumn Festival approaches, what is most worth appreciating is that the full moon in the long sky shines brightly throughout the nine continents, crystal clear and bright. One never tires of leaning on the railing to gaze at it hundreds of times. Here, ancient authors' beautiful verses praising the moon often use elegant characters. I have extracted some examples below to bring a smile to your face.

Jade Wheel (Yuan Ji's poem): The Yellow Road's jade wheel is majestic.

Toad and Hare (Ancient poem): Four or five toads and hares are waning.

Jade Toad (Liu Xiaochuo's poem): Half a jade toad is clustered in the branches.

Golden Hare (Jiang Zong's poem): The golden hare still hangs its soul, the bronze dragon is about to open its door.

Jade Plate (Li Bai's poem): When I was young, I didn't know the moon and called it a white jade plate.

Ice Wheel (Su Shi's poem): The ice wheel rises from the missing snow peak.

Cassia Soul (Wang Wei's poem): The cassia soul is just born, and the autumn dew is slight.

Silver Hare (Emperor Yang of Sui's poem): Clear dew coldly invades the silver hare's shadow. (Qiulang)

Mooncake Song

— (Ni Gaofeng)

The Mid-Autumn Festival, the moon's shape is round, shining on the human world with exceptional freshness, the mooncake is as round as the moon. Its quality is beautiful and its color is gorgeous, every household buys them, competing to be first. In this vast world, amidst the sea of karma, the rise and fall of careers are like floating clouds. It's best to enjoy today's wine and not worry about the transformations of the world. Hoping only to spend time in peace and joy, wishing for this reunion moon to be round every day, and for the fresh and beautiful flowers to be gorgeous every day, even neglecting the pitiful farmers' sweat that drips into the soil. Celebrating the autumn scenery while lamenting the lack of money, staring blankly at the beautiful moon in the sky, just craving the mooncake in front of you, but merely quenching thirst with plums. Hearing the sounds of moon appreciation from the east neighbor, that group's voices are noisy and bustling, and also hearing the sounds of moon appreciation from the west neighbor, holding wine glasses and filled with joy. How different is prosperity from decay, separated like heaven and earth. If we talk about the people in the city eating mooncakes and celebrating reunion, it is even more sincere than the villagers, with fine wine and delicious dishes and lavish feasts, the cakes are as big as basins and filled with all kinds of fruits, cutting and eating them with smiling faces, inviting relatives and friends to dine together, or narrating family reunion, shouting loudly, happy and joyful, the Mid-Autumn Festival is truly not in vain. Moreover, there are those low-ranking officials and subordinates, taking advantage of this time, to spend two hundred silver dollars, buying a big mooncake to send to the powerful and influential top officials, whether it is a yellow box or not, bribes and bribery are irrelevant, hoping everyone understands, from then on the position is solid and firm, maintaining it year after year, the principle of dealing with the world is actually like this, I want to be silent, truly pitiful, if you don't act like this and deal carefully, it is difficult to guarantee that the position will not change, the moon shape is round, the mooncake shape is the same as the bright moon, it turns out it is such a fate.

Miscellaneous words.

New Words on Mid-Autumn

— Aimei

Last year's Mid-Autumn, I wrote trivial words; in a flash, the festival is approaching again. The full tree of osmanthus fragrance, is still strong, a sky of moonlight, as bright as silk; I have abandoned the pen to sell articles, and I am still the same as before. What is slightly different is that before I lived in the countryside, now I am in Shanghai. "Wandering for thousands of miles has become a long-term traveler, and another year easily brings the autumn wind;" reciting Lu You's poem, how can one not feel moved? "Alone in a foreign land as a stranger, on every festive occasion, I think even more of my relatives;" chanting Wang Wei's line, one is even more melancholy!

I have always criticized the idea of spending holidays as meaningless, but I particularly love the Mid-Autumn Festival; this is because I love the moon, and the Mid-Autumn Festival is precisely in the middle of the autumn season, the sky is high and the air is clear, the clouds are light and the wind is clear, making it the most suitable time for admiring the moon, and the moon is indeed more lovely than at other times! If the Moon Sister knows, she will consider me an understanding friend.

The title of Moon Sister, some people think it is based on the story of Chang'e, but in fact it is not; according to the Spring and Autumn Chronicles of Spiritual Omens, "The ruler of men, fathers heaven, mothers earth, brothers sun, sisters moon," its source is probably from this. Especially because the two words "Moon Sister" are fragrant and beautiful beyond compare, so they are most widely spread among the population.

Shen Zi said, "The moon is like a silver pill, receiving the sun's light;" it can be seen that the idea has been around since ancient times, due to the words of Western scientists; according to my research, today's science and our old books often match, this is just one example.

Ancient customs: the day before Mid-Autumn, people make "eye-brighteners" with brocade colors, and give them to each other as gifts; this is probably due to the story of Deng Shao. The Continued Harmonious Records of Qi states, "Shao, on the first day of the eighth month, entered Mount Hua and saw a child holding five-colored ropes, receiving dew on cypress leaves; Shao asked: What is this for? The child replied: Master Chisong takes it to brighten his eyes." Later generations imitate this and it became a custom. There are also those who do it on the first day of the month. The Record of Telling about Conquests says, "On the first day of the eighth month, make five bright ropes, take the dew from the tops of a hundred grasses to wash the eyes, so that the eyes will be bright." Also, they use vermilion water to dot the heads and foreheads of children, called "heavenly branding," to ward off diseases; also on the day before Mid-Autumn, all seen in the Seasonal Records of Jingchu.

According to the Miscellaneous Morsels from Youyang, "In the country of Polozhe, on the fifteenth day of the eighth month, they perform statues and tightrope walking for entertainment;" the strange people and customs can be a joke. However, where exactly this country of Polozhe is, I have not been able to examine; is it perhaps a utopia? It also says, "During the Changqing era, someone playing with the moon on the fifteenth night of the eighth month, the light belonged to the forest, the middle was like a bolt of cloth, and looking for it, they saw a golden-backed toad: the matter is also strange and absurd. I mean, perhaps it is still just a rural tale of Qi."

The Mid-Autumn moon has a different name, called the "Upright First Month." Therefore, Han Changli's poem says, "The Upright First Month of the three autumns, comes out of the eastern sea tonight." I say, its name is certainly not bad, but it feels somewhat stuffy, and the wording makes me feel like it is too upright. A laugh!

The legend of Emperor Xuanzong of the Tang Dynasty and Master Shen, the Taoist Hongdu guest, touring the Guanghan Palace on Mid-Autumn night is quite popular; the Rainbow Feather Robe Dance composed for it was not passed down to the world, and those who speak of it regret it. And they do not know that in ancient Yuefu music, there was the Song of a Widow, probably composed by the Han people when there was no moon during Mid-Autumn; Li He's Eighth Month Music poem has the line: "The widowed concubine resents the long night," which refers to this. It was also lost, truly regrettable.

"When will the bright moon be there? I hold my wine to ask the blue sky. I don't know what year it is tonight in the palaces in the sky? I want to ride the wind to return, but I fear the high palaces in the jade towers cannot withstand the cold. I rise to dance with my clear shadow, how is it like being in the human world? Turning to the red pavilion, lowering to the patterned door, shining on those who cannot sleep. There should be no resentment, why is it round only at the time of parting? People have sorrow, joy, separation, and reunion, the moon has gloom, brightness, fullness, and wane, such things are difficult to perfect since ancient times. I only wish people will be long-lived, and share the beauty of the moon from a thousand miles away." This is the Su Dongpo Water Melody Prelude that is widely recited in the literary world. According to Dongpo, Zhu Jiayou was a Jinshi scholar, but during the reign of Emperor Shenzong, his opinions clashed with Wang Anshi, and he was demoted to Huangzhou. On the Mid-Autumn of the Bingchen year, he drank happily until dawn, and thus filled in this poem. At that time, it spread throughout the capital, and the eunuch recorded this and presented it to the emperor. Emperor Shenzong read until "but I fear the high palaces in the jade towers cannot withstand the cold," and said: Su Shi still loves the ruler, and then ordered him to be transferred to Ruzhou. This is also an old fact of Mid-Autumn that one should know.

The most common of Mid-Autumn foods is the mooncake, and those who eat cake are rare, but there was such a custom in the past; the Yuan Family Side Courtyard Record says, "On the night of Mid-Autumn, Emperor Wuzong and the concubines ate the moonflower cake." The cake is called moonflower, how elegant! Moreover, the cake is mostly made of glutinous rice flour, and if made properly, its taste is even more delicious than mooncakes; from now on, on Mid-Autumn, it may be worthwhile to repeat the story of Emperor Wuzong, to promote eating it.

Other seasonal foods, such as water chestnuts, lotus roots, chestnuts, persimmons, apples, lilies, pomegranates, taro, etc. are all good. There is also a kind of lotus root cake, made by mashing fresh lotus root, mixing it with rice flour, taking osmanthus-flavored oil to make a cake, making it into a cake shape, and frying it in oil. It is delicious and moist, and I like it most; unfortunately, I am now a guest, and cannot get to eat it; thinking of this makes me even more homesick.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

It's Mid-Autumn Again

— Fang Kewen

Another year easily passes, it's Mid-Autumn again.

Mid-Autumn is an important event in commerce. Personnel changes mostly happen on this day. Compared to the end of the year, its importance is not much less. In this era when the wave of economic recession is relentlessly striking, and China's national industry is under the heavy pressure of foreign capital, we really dare not speculate on how many factories and shops will quietly declare liquidation under this "festival checkpoint", and how many personnel will lose their jobs due to retrenchment? And this year, because of the rampant smuggling, we dare not imagine what the situation will be even after passing Mid-Autumn.

Mid-Autumn is also the season that most easily stirs up the sorrows of travelers. The ancient poet's line "The moon is curved, shining on the nine provinces, some families happy, some families sorrowful" has already spoken for us the feelings of travelers. This line, which was recited for a time and known to every household, was written by ancient people. Now, we witness the changing colors of the mountains and rivers (it's already been five years!), and the national crisis is deepening day by day, our feelings are certainly not limited to this!

The Mid-Autumn moon is the brightest moon of the year, and we cannot help but be moved when we look at it. We are still the people hiding in this corner of Shanghai, where we are making merry and celebrating peace. Although we have already seen the brutal face of the enemy, and the pain of the resulting industrial and commercial decline, compared to those who live under the iron heel, or who have fled from under the iron heel, the "homeless" people, we have a little less "personal" pain. However, we are already overwhelmed by the taste of "the country is broken, but the mountains and rivers remain"; if the "homeless" people who are "drifting abroad" and the people struggling under the iron heel see this bright moonlight, thinking of the Changbai Mountains, and "the world's first pass" where "the scenery is still the same", what kind of grief will they have?

Shanghai is superficially a world of making merry and celebrating peace, but if we tear off its extravagant coat and look at the essence inside, we really don't have the courage to be optimistic; these few days, especially because of the sudden outbreak of the unfortunate incident on Haining Road, the situation has become very tense, and people are panicked, with a great momentum of not being able to last even a day, making us dare not imagine what kind of face this Shanghai, drunk on money, will become?

Page 20

Festival

— Shen Jiaqian

The bill collecting clerk, like an old horse that has unloaded a heavy load, stepped into the shop, put his black leather briefcase on the counter, and collapsed into the armchair, just wiping the sweat from his brow with his handkerchief. Seeing a cup of cold tea on the counter, he grabbed it and gulped it down his throat before opening his mouth to speak:

"Each festival is worse than the last! Out of eight hundred-odd debts, I only collected two hundred-odd dollars!"

He opened his briefcase, counted the bills, and handed them to the manager, along with a stack of invoices for outstanding debts.

The manager seemed to be bewitched. Since the clerk left to collect debts after dinner, he had used the abacus several times. Pharmacies were originally the most profitable businesses, buying goods by the catty and selling them by the fen and qian; of course, one couldn't keep all the profits to oneself by making loans. Usually, offering an 80% or 90% discount, a profit of 40% was still guaranteed. Although the year was economically depressed, people still got sick. From the Dragon Boat Festival to Mid-Autumn, eight hundred-odd debts could be considered good business. But when the manager put the abacus to use, his eyeballs seemed stuck on the beads, almost unable to move. Even if all eight hundred-odd debts were collected with an 80% or 90% discount, it would only be enough to recoup his original capital. The interest was all spent on advertising and all kinds of giveaways.

"Making a sale is so difficult these days!" The manager couldn't help scratching his scalp with his long fingernails, pacing back and forth in the small space in front of the loan counter.

Across the street, a sugar and vegetable store had just put up a colorful archway, hiring several wind and percussion musicians to make a racket all morning. The sunlight shone on the center of the street, and the electric lights spelling out "Twelfth Anniversary" were already lit. When the manager looked up, his eyes felt as if they were being pricked by needles.

"Damn it!" His resentment found a place to vent. "Everything's on sale year-round, is it really the twelfth anniversary? Don't tell me all these shameless... What kind of great sale does a pharmacy have? Poor people shouldn't get sick. If they can afford to be sick, are they afraid of losing their lives? Doctors, pharmacies, this is a tougher business than the coffin shop! Shameless, they come up with these big sales with reduced prices, printing a full page of advertisements, putting up electric light archways, giving away tiger bone and papaya wine, so you also reduce prices, I also reduce prices, and Yanshou Hall, a centuries-old shop, fell down in one festival..."

Thinking about Yanshou Hall falling down, the manager saw countless gold flies buzzing in front of his eyes. But he barely managed to calm himself and sat down again to use the abacus. He made many calculations. For example, if he could collect six hundred dollars out of eight hundred-odd debts, he could barely get through Mid-Autumn. The end of the year was the most profitable time of year. Sick people needed medicine, and healthy people needed tonics. The Wang residence, the Li residence, ginseng and silver ear fungus, each order was three hundred or five hundred dollars. As long as he could hold onto these few residences, was he still afraid of falling down?

A glimmer of hope finally appeared before the manager's eyes. He waited for the bill collecting clerk to bring back hope, flipping through the account books and puffing on his pipe, occasionally casting a disdainful glance at the colorful archway across the street to show his defiance.

When the bill collecting clerk returned, the shop had already had dinner. The manager was just using his goose feather tube to pick the rice grains left in his teeth. He often complained about his toothache and often said that when he got a bonus, he would have the dentist fix his whole mouth because taking care of one's body was important.

Now the clerk was sitting in the armchair across from him, with two hundred-odd dollars in bills in front of him. His whole body felt electrified. He slowly reached out to grab that stack of invoices, the first one being from the Li residence. This big customer's outstanding bill was two hundred and forty-eight dollars.

"What!" He widened his eyes at the clerk. "You didn't collect anything from the Li residence either?"

The clerk nodded, but the manager's eyes didn't leave his face, and he spoke in the smallest voice.

"Their whole family has gone to Qingdao. The old nanny who often came with Mrs. Li told me that Master Li lost over two million in the stock exchange, and they might have to sell their house."

The manager sat down. His hands trembled as he flipped through the invoices, one by one. The gold flies buzzed in front of his eyes again in droves, gradually making it hard to see the numbers on the invoices. But those numbers had already taken root in his stomach—over eight hundred dollars!

After the Autumn Harvest

— Li Xuan

The old woman, carrying a copper kettle, walked in. As soon as she entered, she turned her face to the Second Master and said:

"Mr. Hu said Zhenping is back. Please, Second Master, go have a look at the grain."

The Second Master grunted, threw the cigarette butt from the corner of his mouth into the spittoon, and walked towards the courtyard.

The row of Rouge Red in the courtyard had been blown bare by the autumn wind, the yellow-green leaves mixed with pale red petals covered the muddy ground in the row, and many black seed pods of jasmine were blown by the wind, rolling on the brick ground. The Second Master walked into the accounting room, wiped the corner of his mouth with a handkerchief, and the two middle-aged men beside the table stood up.

The Second Master sat in the chair of honor by the window, looking at Zhenping standing at the corner of the table opposite him, and said:

"Haven't you eaten?"

"No hurry, Second Master, take a look at this." This middle-aged man was very satisfying to the Shu family. He himself ran a small general store on the south street of this town, letting his brother take care of it. But he bought grain for the Second Master at various docks, lending money with a reliable guarantor. He was quite astute in every way and had a bit of eloquence. At this time, he pushed the three paper packages on the table over and pointed to the first package:

"This 'Big Snake Eye' (red-hatted sorghum with large grains) is really good, Second Master, take a bite. It's 'ice areca nut mouth' (meaning crisp and dry). We collected 150 dan of it. That's old dou. Combined with our new dou (measuring unit) here, it's 340 with a little change."

"What price?"

"This one is five dollars and eighty cents." He pushed the first package next to the abacus, then pulled the second package over: "This one is a bit worse in quality, three dollars and twenty cents. We didn't collect much of this. Overall, the sorghum, no matter the quality, averages out to four dollars and ten cents per dan, including the porterage and miscellaneous expenses. Right now, the market price here is...?"

The accountant, Mr. Hu, who had been silent for a long time and had retreated to sit by the table, was listening honestly. He calculated that the purchased grain was just over four dollars per dan. There was little rice collected from the market, but a lot of cotton could be sold... Suddenly, he saw his assistant looking at him questioningly, so he anxiously said:

"The high price is four dollars and sixty or seventy cents."

Then the Second Master's eyes also turned to look at him, and he smartly sat up straight.

The man who had been reporting grain prices for a long time walked over and poured two cups of tea from the kettle on the table, very respectfully placing one bowl in front of the master.

"Second Master, won't you have a drink?"

The Second Master watched him drink several bowls of tea in a row, then opened the third paper package on the table himself. Inside was a large handful of plump wheat kernels.

"What's the price of this wheat?"

"Wheat is really scarce," he shouted loudly, spattering saliva onto the table. The master glared at him, and he withdrew his hand, which he had been waving in the air: "We only bought fifty-six dan. It was agreed to be seventy-eight cents, but who knew the Hongchang family on West Street also went to buy it! They offered eighty-two cents, and they snatched seventy dan away. I immediately lost my temper. How can you do business like that? We're almost 'over the dou' (meaning making a loss), and the people in the dou bureau said nice things and asked us to be understanding..."

The Second Master was a little displeased. He knew that local wheat sold for ninety-seven or ninety-eight cents. The Cold Dew solar term had already passed, and not a drop of rain had fallen. No one could sow wheat, so if he could hoard three or four hundred dan, he would make a fortune next spring. How could he let someone else take seventy dan with a higher price! So he said:

Page 21

Shanghai Postal Administration Mail Dispatch Schedule

All branches in Shanghai can send registered express airmail and handle remittances, savings, and other services.

Page 22

Page 23

"Didn't you receive my letter?"

"No!"

"Sigh," he patted his thigh regretfully, "Eighty-two cents is still worth it!"

The man, because he had talked for so long, was very excited and his face was red. After being told this by the master, he knew that the local wheat had risen again, and he felt that the master was a little unhappy. So he took out the "flower bill" for buying grain from his waist, pointed and told the master how much grain each family had and how much money they got. Finally, he said:

"The rules of the dou bureau are: pay when the grain arrives!"

The Second Master nodded and, as if doting on a child, told him to go to the kitchen to get something to eat. The man then quietly slipped out of the room.

At this time, there was a banging sound in the courtyard. Little Qiu and Lao Chun were carrying kerosene into the east wing. The Second Master watched through the window as they quickly finished arranging the barrels, then said to the accountant:

"Go tell Bu Lao San that the forty-three dollars for kerosene will be added to the rent."

The accountant grunted in agreement and walked into the courtyard. Little Qiu was unlocking the door there. Seeing the accountant come out, he jumped down the steps and shouted:

"Mr. Hu, write down forty-five dollars for Bu Lao San's kerosene."

Mr. Hu was caught off guard by the child's sharp shout, and his ears rang slightly. He pressed his ear with a finger and said:

"The master said forty-three."

"It's gone up again. The supply isn't coming down from above. Tomorrow a barrel will sell for five dollars."

Mr. Hu turned his head and looked at the master sticking his head out of the glass window, as if to say: What should we do?

The Second Master waved his hand in the room, saying in a hoarse voice:

"Forty-five it is. Tell him we'll add it to the rent!"

Mr. Hu coughed and shrugged his shoulders, quickly walking out of the courtyard.

Zhongxi (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening: "Mid-Autumn Moon Difficult"

Year after year, seasons come and go. The sun and moon rush by like flowing water. This year's autumn moon is still present. This year, the eighth month has arrived again. Thinking of today, the Mid-Autumn Festival on the fifteenth of the month, I only see a round bright moon shining on tall buildings. The clouds are faint, and the full moon adds charm. I can't help but imitate Emperor Ming and ascend to the moon. Oh, moon, I see that today your face is different from before. I see that your desolate color is all gone. I see that your beautiful and full splendor seems to be smiling. I see that it is all because every family is celebrating the moon without end. I see that although you are clear and bright like a mirror. I see that moonlight cannot solve people's sorrows. Do you know, some families happily admire the moon together. Some families sadly face the moon in loneliness. Some families see the moon with sad faces. Some families love the moon and go out to enjoy it. Some are husbands and wives spending their honeymoon together. Some are living in the East and West, each plotting their own course. Some are gathering under the moon to feast together. Some are rushing about everywhere, running around all their lives. Some are happily and freely inviting the full moon. Some are wandering about, unable to be free. Some are like the Mid-Autumn moon. Some are like the crescent moon hook. I think that the full moon will inevitably wane. Even the crescent moon is still afraid of being imprisoned by clouds. How can mortals compare to the great void of the moon? In the end, the moon in the mirror is all illusory. The moon wanes but has a day to be full again. How can a person who dies return like the moon? The moon wanes and waxes year after year. How can a human life be as long as the moon's? How can one share eternity with the moon?

Movie News

Zhou Xuan Surrounded by Male and Female Students

The Yi Hua new film "Happiness at the Door" is currently filming outdoor scenes in Huishan, Wuxi. There are fifty or sixty people going together. They get up at six o'clock every day, practice sports, and at seven o'clock, they are busy filming. Residents in Wuxi urban and rural areas are curious and rush to watch the excitement. The number of people watching often exceeds a thousand. The Thirty-sixth Division of the garrison is afraid of incidents and sends a team to protect them. The situation is magnificent. There are also many male and female students who come to find Zhou Xuan every day, surrounding her and asking her to sign autographs. Sometimes she feels that her hand is tired.

Grand Shanghai Grand Theater Presents the Colorful Blockbuster "Buccaneer in Silk"

The film industry's first three-color, stereoscopic, colorful song and dance blockbuster, "Buccaneer in Silk," will be presented at the Grand Shanghai Grand Theater starting today. The film stars Corinne Collins and Stephen "The Gay Deception" Dunne, with support from the master of humor, Frank Morgan. The film features five or six song and dance scenes, with the Spanish castanet dance and the Carabe dance being the most exciting. The actors' costumes are extremely beautiful and moving. Coupled with the rendering of colors, it is even more radiant, dazzling, and unmatched. It is rumored that RKO spent nearly three million gold dollars to produce the film.

"Anthony Adverse" Opens Today

Background Spanning Five Continents, Over Four Hundred Scenes

Warner Brothers, after spending more than two years and exerting all its efforts to produce "Anthony Adverse," is now showing it in advance at the Grand Theater starting today (Wednesday). The completion of this literary film has shocked the entire Hollywood film industry, and they all believe that this is the biggest harvest of the film industry this year. In terms of achievements in film art, it is more remarkable than "A Midsummer Night's Dream" and other films.

The film tells the story of a girl, Maria, who is forced by a snobbish father to marry the old and declining Marquis Don Luis, and has a physical relationship with her old lover, the Irish military officer Moore. She becomes pregnant and they agree to elope to Canada. Unfortunately, Don discovers them, and in a sword fight, Moore dies by the sword. After Maria gives birth, she also dies miserably. Don sends the child to a monastery. It happens to be the feast day of St. Anthony, so the priest names him Anthony. When Anthony is - years old, he is sent to Bonafé (Maria's father) to study. Bonafé, through special hidden knowledge, learns that he is his grandson, and cherishes him to the fullest, keeping it a secret. This charmer, from childhood to adulthood, has fallen in love with three women. One of them, Angela, also becomes pregnant. Later, she joins the Teatro de la República opera troupe and her reputation grows daily. Later, she even becomes a favorite captive of Napoleon. Until Anthony returns from Africa and wants to rekindle their old love, he suddenly discovers their illegitimate child. The King Napoleon, knowing the truth, sends Anthony as an envoy to the United States. The whole film ends with Anthony taking the third generation of little Anthony, echoing the title of the film, as a sail vaguely disappears into the distance.

When the film was about to start shooting, the adaptation of the script and the selection of actors had already taken a lot of time and deliberation. And because the area in the story includes five continents, and the time spans twenty-five years, they must be carefully researched and cannot be fabricated. The nationality, personality, and age of each character in the book must be clearly analyzed. As a result, after two years, ninety-eight important actors were selected, and four hundred scenes were built. Then the director, Mervyn LeRoy, began to spend months of effort to introduce this famous novel "Anthony Adverse," which has three million readers, to the screen. This is indeed an unparalleled glory in the film industry.
